// src/types/mission-filter.types.ts

export type WMoonFactorKey =
  | 'x1_skillMatch'
  | 'x2_timeEfficiency'
  | 'x3_successProbability'
  | 'x4_scam'
  | 'x5_growth'
  | 'x6_utility'
  | 'x7_urgency'
  | 'x8_consistency'
  | 'x9_trust';

export type WMoonWeights = Record<WMoonFactorKey, number>;

export interface UserAIProfileRow {
  user_id: string;
  skill_vector: Record<string, number> | null;
  weights: WMoonWeights | null;
  learning_rate: number;
  risk_tolerance: number;
  beta_stats: { alpha: number; beta: number } | null;
  last_updated: string;
}

export interface UserRow {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  full_name: string | null;
  created_at: string;
  last_active_at: string;
  status: 'active' | 'banned' | 'inactive';
}

export interface UserMissionHistoryRow {
  id: string;
  user_id: string;
  mission_id: string;
  action: 'viewed' | 'accepted' | 'rejected' | 'completed' | 'hidden';
  feedback_rating: number | null;
  action_timestamp: string;
}

export interface MissionFilterRow {
  id: string;
  mission_id: string;
  user_id: string;
  total_score: number;
  factors_breakdown: Record<string, number>;
  is_scam: boolean;
  scam_reason: string | null;
  calculated_at: string;
}

export interface AIAuditLogRow {
  id: string;
  user_id: string;
  mission_id: string;
  decision_type: 'SCAM_BLOCK' | 'HIGH_SCORE' | 'WEIGHT_UPDATE' | 'INFO';
  explanation: string;
  snapshot_weights: WMoonWeights | null;
  created_at: string;
}

/**
 * Missione "raw" che arriva dal tuo sistema (scraping, input manuale, ecc.)
 * Prima della normalizzazione NLP.
 */
export interface RawMissionInput {
  id: string; // id interno del tuo sistema (non db uuid obbligatorio)
  title: string;
  description: string;
  sourceUrl?: string;
  rewardAmount: number;
  estimatedHours: number;
  deadline: Date;
  sourceId: string; // es. job board, sito, referenza
}

/**
 * Missione arricchita dal layer NLP + normalizzazione
 * (usata dal motore di scoring W-MOON).
 */
export interface NormalizedMission {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  category: string; // es. 'coding', 'writing'
  skills: string[];
  rewardAmount: number;
  estimatedHours: number;
  difficulty: number; // 1–10
  cognitiveLoad: number; // 0–10
  physicalLoad: number; // 0–10
  deadline: Date;
  sourceId: string;
}

/**
 * Dati dell’utente necessari per W-MOON (aggregati da varie tabelle).
 */
export interface UserScoringContext {
  userId: string;
  skills: Set<string>;
  avgHourlyRate: number;
  skillLevel: number; // 1–10
  lastActiveAt: Date;
  streakCount: number;
  hasHistory: boolean;
  successes: number;
  failures: number;
  trustMap: Record<string, number>; // sourceId -> trust score (0–1)
  weights: WMoonWeights;
  learningRate: number;
}

/**
 * Output finale per il frontend / consumer dell’API.
 */
export interface FilteredMission {
  missionId: string;
  userId: string;
  totalScore: number;
  isScam: boolean;
  scamReason?: string;
  factors: Record<WMoonFactorKey, number>;
  reasoning: string; // breve spiegazione leggibile
  normalizedMission: NormalizedMission;
}
2. src/utils/scoring-functions.ts
Qui portiamo l’algoritmo W-MOON in TS, con funzioni riusabili.

// src/utils/scoring-functions.ts

import {
  NormalizedMission,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
  WMoonFactorKey,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';

const GLOBAL_ALPHA = 5;
const GLOBAL_BETA = 5;

/**
 * Keywords base per rilevare truffe.
 */
export const DEFAULT_SCAM_KEYWORDS = [
  'telegram',
  'whatsapp',
  'security fee',
  'deposit',
  'gift card',
];

export interface WMoonScoreResult {
  score: number; // 0–100
  isScam: boolean;
  scamReason?: string;
  factors: Record<WMoonFactorKey, number>;
}

export function getDefaultWeights(): WMoonWeights {
  return {
    x1_skillMatch: 0.15,
    x2_timeEfficiency: 0.15,
    x3_successProbability: 0.1,
    x4_scam: 0.2,
    x5_growth: 0.1,
    x6_utility: 0.1,
    x7_urgency: 0.1,
    x8_consistency: 0.05,
    x9_trust: 0.05,
  };
}

// ---------- FATTORI W-MOON (x1–x9) ----------

export function skillMatchScore(
  userSkills: Set<string>,
  missionSkills: string[],
): number {
  const missionSet = new Set(missionSkills);
  const intersection = [...missionSet].filter((s) => userSkills.has(s)).length;
  const union = new Set([...userSkills, ...missionSet]).size;
  if (union === 0) return 0;
  return intersection / union; // Jaccard
}

export function timeEfficiencyScore(
  reward: number,
  estHours: number,
  userAvgRate: number,
): number {
  if (estHours <= 0) return 0;
  const roti = reward / estHours; // Return on Time Invested
  const avgRate = userAvgRate > 0 ? userAvgRate : 15.0;
  const k = 0.5;
  const v = 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-k * (roti - avgRate)));
  return clamp01(v);
}

export function successProbabilityScore(
  hasHistory: boolean,
  successes: number,
  failures: number,
): number {
  const alpha = hasHistory ? successes || 0 : GLOBAL_ALPHA;
  const beta = hasHistory ? failures || 0 : GLOBAL_BETA;
  if (alpha + beta === 0) return 0.5;
  return alpha / (alpha + beta);
}

export function scamDetectionScore(
  mission: NormalizedMission,
  scamKeywords: string[] = DEFAULT_SCAM_KEYWORDS,
): { score: number; isScam: boolean; reason?: string } {
  let riskScore = 0;
  const textBody = `${mission.title} ${mission.description}`.toLowerCase();
  const reasons: string[] = [];

  // Rule 1: keywords
  for (const kw of scamKeywords) {
    if (textBody.includes(kw.toLowerCase())) {
      riskScore += 1.0;
      reasons.push(`keyword sospetta: "${kw}"`);
    }
  }

  // Rule 2: reward troppo alta / effort troppo basso
  if (mission.rewardAmount > 200 && mission.estimatedHours < 0.5) {
    riskScore += 0.8;
    reasons.push('reward molto alta con effort minimo');
  }

  const x4 = clamp01(1 - riskScore);
  const isScam = x4 < 0.2;
  const reason = isScam ? reasons.join(' | ') || 'pattern sospetto rilevato' : undefined;

  return { score: x4, isScam, reason };
}

export function personalGrowthScore(
  userSkillLevel: number,
  missionDifficulty: number,
): number {
  const gap = missionDifficulty - userSkillLevel;
  const optimalGap = 1.0;
  const sigma = 1.5;
  const exponent = -((gap - optimalGap) ** 2) / (2 * sigma ** 2);
  return clamp01(Math.exp(exponent));
}

export function utilityScore(
  reward: number,
  cognitiveLoad: number,
  physicalLoad: number,
): number {
  const effort = cognitiveLoad + physicalLoad;
  const num = Math.log(1 + Math.max(reward, 0));
  const den = Math.log(1 + effort + 1);
  if (!isFinite(num) || !isFinite(den) || den === 0) return 0;
  const v = num / den;
  return clamp01(v);
}

export function urgencyScore(deadline: Date, now: Date): number {
  const hoursLeft =
    (deadline.getTime() - now.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60);
  if (!isFinite(hoursLeft)) return 0;
  const threshold = 24;
  const k = 0.2;
  const v = 1 / (1 + Math.exp(k * (hoursLeft - threshold)));
  return clamp01(v);
}

export function consistencyScore(streakCount: number): number {
  const v = Math.tanh(0.1 * streakCount);
  return clamp01(v);
}

export function trustScore(trustMap: Record<string, number>, sourceId: string): number {
  const v = trustMap[sourceId] ?? 0.5;
  return clamp01(v);
}

// ---------- AGGREGAZIONE W-MOON ----------

export function calculateWMoonScore(
  user: UserScoringContext,
  mission: NormalizedMission,
  weights: WMoonWeights,
  now: Date,
): WMoonScoreResult {
  const x1 = skillMatchScore(user.skills, mission.skills);
  const x2 = timeEfficiencyScore(
    mission.rewardAmount,
    mission.estimatedHours,
    user.avgHourlyRate,
  );
  const x3 = successProbabilityScore(
    user.hasHistory,
    user.successes,
    user.failures,
  );
  const scamResult = scamDetectionScore(mission);
  const x4 = scamResult.score;
  const x5 = personalGrowthScore(user.skillLevel, mission.difficulty);
  const x6 = utilityScore(
    mission.rewardAmount,
    mission.cognitiveLoad,
    mission.physicalLoad,
  );
  const x7 = urgencyScore(mission.deadline, now);
  const x8 = consistencyScore(user.streakCount);
  const x9 = trustScore(user.trustMap, mission.sourceId);

  const factors: Record<WMoonFactorKey, number> = {
    x1_skillMatch: round2(x1),
    x2_timeEfficiency: round2(x2),
    x3_successProbability: round2(x3),
    x4_scam: round2(x4),
    x5_growth: round2(x5),
    x6_utility: round2(x6),
    x7_urgency: round2(x7),
    x8_consistency: round2(x8),
    x9_trust: round2(x9),
  };

  // Gatekeeper sicurezza
  if (x4 < 0.2) {
    return {
      score: 0,
      isScam: true,
      scamReason: scamResult.reason ?? 'Sicurezza troppo bassa',
      factors,
    };
  }

  const raw =
    x1 * weights.x1_skillMatch +
    x2 * weights.x2_timeEfficiency +
    x3 * weights.x3_successProbability +
    x4 * weights.x4_scam +
    x5 * weights.x5_growth +
    x6 * weights.x6_utility +
    x7 * weights.x7_urgency +
    x8 * weights.x8_consistency +
    x9 * weights.x9_trust;

  const score = clamp01(raw) * 100;

  return {
    score: round1(score),
    isScam: false,
    factors,
  };
}

// ---------- LEARNING / UPDATE PESI ----------

export function updateWMoonWeights(
  weights: WMoonWeights,
  factors: Record<WMoonFactorKey, number>,
  finalScore: number, // 0–100
  action: 1 | -1, // 1 = accepted/completed, -1 = rejected/hidden
  learningRate: number,
): WMoonWeights {
  const predicted = clamp01(finalScore / 100);
  const actual = action === 1 ? 1 : 0;
  const error = actual - predicted;

  const entries = Object.entries(weights) as [WMoonFactorKey, number][];
  const updated: Partial<WMoonWeights> = {};

  for (const [key, w] of entries) {
    const factorVal = factors[key] ?? 0;
    const delta = learningRate * error * factorVal;
    updated[key] = w + delta;
  }

  // Rinormalizza a somma = 1
  const sum = Object.values(updated).reduce(
    (acc, v) => acc + (v ?? 0),
    0,
  );
  const normalized: WMoonWeights = {} as WMoonWeights;
  for (const [key, v] of Object.entries(updated) as [
    WMoonFactorKey,
    number,
  ][]) {
    normalized[key] = sum > 0 ? v / sum : 1 / 9;
  }

  // Hard constraint: non far scendere troppo la sicurezza
  normalized.x4_scam = Math.max(normalized.x4_scam, 0.15);

  return normalized;
}

// ---------- HELPERS ----------

function clamp01(v: number): number {
  if (!isFinite(v)) return 0;
  if (v < 0) return 0;
  if (v > 1) return 1;
  return v;
}

function round2(v: number): number {
  return Math.round(v * 100) / 100;
}

function round1(v: number): number {
  return Math.round(v * 10) / 10;
}
3. src/services/ai-profile.service.ts
Service che aggiorna il profilo AI dopo ogni missione.

// src/services/ai-profile.service.ts

import { Kysely } from 'kysely';
import {
  FilteredMission,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserMissionHistoryRow,
  WMoonWeights,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';
import { updateWMoonWeights } from '../utils/scoring-functions';

export type MissionOutcome = 'accepted' | 'rejected' | 'completed' | 'hidden';

interface DB {
  user_ai_profile: UserAIProfileRow;
  user_mission_history: UserMissionHistoryRow;
}

export class UserAIProfileService {
  constructor(private readonly db: Kysely<DB>) {}

  /**
   * Aggiorna il profilo AI dell’utente dopo una decisione su una missione.
   * action:
   *  - accepted/completed => rafforza la configurazione corrente
   *  - rejected/hidden    => penalizza configurazione che ha generato score alto
   */
  async updateProfileAfterMission(
    userId: string,
    mission: FilteredMission,
    outcome: MissionOutcome,
  ): Promise<void> {
    const profile = await this.db
      .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
      .selectAll()
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!profile) {
      // No profile: niente da aggiornare per ora
      return;
    }

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      profile.weights ?? this.getFallbackWeights();
    const learningRate = profile.learning_rate ?? 0.05;

    const action: 1 | -1 =
      outcome === 'accepted' || outcome === 'completed' ? 1 : -1;

    const newWeights = updateWMoonWeights(
      weights,
      mission.factors,
      mission.totalScore,
      action,
      learningRate,
    );

    await this.db
      .updateTable('user_ai_profile')
      .set({
        weights: newWeights,
        last_updated: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .execute();
  }

  private getFallbackWeights(): WMoonWeights {
    return {
      x1_skillMatch: 0.15,
      x2_timeEfficiency: 0.15,
      x3_successProbability: 0.1,
      x4_scam: 0.2,
      x5_growth: 0.1,
      x6_utility: 0.1,
      x7_urgency: 0.1,
      x8_consistency: 0.05,
      x9_trust: 0.05,
    };
  }
}
4. src/services/mission-filter.service.ts
Il cuore: chiama OpenAI per normalizzare la missione, calcola W-MOON, salva nel DB, ritorna al chiamante.

// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import OpenAI from 'openai';
import { Kysely } from 'kysely';
import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserRow,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';
import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from '../utils/scoring-functions';

interface DB {
  users: UserRow;
  user_ai_profile: UserAIProfileRow;
  // missions / mission_filters / ai_audit_log sono nel db reale ma non ci servono tipizzati al 100% qui
}

interface MissionFilterServiceDeps {
  db: Kysely<DB>;
  openai: OpenAI;
  logger?: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
  scamKeywordsOverride?: string[];
}

/**
 * Servizio principale che:
 * - arricchisce le missioni con NLP (OpenAI)
 * - calcola score W-MOON
 * - ordina e ritorna missioni con reasoning
 */
export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: MissionFilterServiceDeps['logger'];

  constructor(deps: MissionFilterServiceDeps) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
  }

  /**
   * Entrypoint principale: prende un utente + lista missioni raw,
   * ritorna missioni filtrate/ordinate con score e reasoning.
   */
  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[],
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (!rawMissions.length) return [];

    const userContext = await this.buildUserContext(userId);

    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m)),
    );

    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];

    const now = new Date();

    for (const mission of normalized) {
      const weights = userContext.weights ?? getDefaultWeights();

      const wmResult = calculateWMoonScore(
        userContext,
        mission,
        weights,
        now,
      );

      const reasoning = this.buildReasoning(mission, wmResult.score, wmResult);

      results.push({
        missionId: mission.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wmResult.score,
        isScam: wmResult.isScam,
        scamReason: wmResult.scamReason,
        factors: wmResult.factors,
        reasoning,
        normalizedMission: mission,
      });
    }

    // ordina per score decrescente, truffe in fondo
    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // ---------- USER CONTEXT ----------

  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom('users')
        .selectAll()
        .where('id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
        .selectAll()
        .where('user_id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) {
      throw new Error(`User ${userId} non trovato`);
    }

    const now = new Date();
    const lastActiveAt = new Date(user.last_active_at);
    const daysSinceActive =
      (now.getTime() - lastActiveAt.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);

    // decadenza skills se molto inattivo, come nel tuo algoritmo
    let skillLevel = profile ? 7 : 5;
    let streakCount = 0;

    if (daysSinceActive > 30 && profile) {
      skillLevel *= 0.9;
      streakCount = 0;
    }

    const skillVector = (profile?.skill_vector ?? {}) as Record<
      string,
      number
    >;

    // skills binarie derivate dal vettore
    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase()),
    );

    // fallback molto semplice per avg rate
    const avgHourlyRate = 30;

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights | null) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    const trustMap: Record<string, number> = {}; // TODO: leggere da tabella separata se/quando serve

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate,
      skillLevel,
      lastActiveAt,
      streakCount,
      hasHistory: false, // TODO: potresti leggere da user_mission_history
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap,
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // ---------- NLP NORMALIZATION (OpenAI) ----------

  /**
   * Usa OpenAI (gpt-3.5-turbo) per:
   * - estrarre categoria
   * - estrarre skills richieste
   * - stimare difficulty, cognitive/physical load
   */
  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput,
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const systemPrompt = `
Sei un assistente che normalizza offerte di lavoro / missioni freelance.
Devi restituire SOLO JSON valido con questa struttura:

{
  "category": "coding" | "writing" | "design" | "admin" | "other",
  "skills": string[], 
  "difficulty": number,        // 1-10
  "cognitiveLoad": number,     // 0-10
  "physicalLoad": number       // 0-10
}
`;

    const userPrompt = `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore stimate: ${raw.estimatedHours}
Fonte: ${raw.sourceUrl ?? 'n/a'}
`;

    try {
      const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: 'gpt-3.5-turbo',
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
          { role: 'user', content: userPrompt },
        ],
      });

      const content =
        completion.choices[0].message?.content?.trim() ?? '{}';

      let parsed: any;
      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(content);
      } catch (err) {
        this.logger?.error(
          '[MissionFilterService] JSON parsing fallito, uso fallback:',
          err,
          content,
        );
        parsed = {};
      }

      const category =
        typeof parsed.category === 'string' ? parsed.category : 'other';

      const skills: string[] = Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
        ? parsed.skills.map((s: unknown) => String(s).toLowerCase())
        : [];

      const difficulty = normalizeNumber(parsed.difficulty, 5, 1, 10);
      const cognitiveLoad = normalizeNumber(
        parsed.cognitiveLoad,
        5,
        0,
        10,
      );
      const physicalLoad = normalizeNumber(
        parsed.physicalLoad,
        1,
        0,
        10,
      );

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category,
        skills,
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty,
        cognitiveLoad,
        physicalLoad,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger?.error(
        '[MissionFilterService] Errore NLP, uso fallback naive:',
        err,
      );

      // fallback “hard-coded” se l’AI fallisce
      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: 'other',
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // ---------- REASONING ----------

  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wmResult: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>,
  ): string {
    const f = wmResult.factors;
    const highlights: string[] = [];

    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) {
      highlights.push('forte match con le tue skill');
    }
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7) {
      highlights.push('ottimo rapporto paga/tempo');
    }
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) {
      highlights.push('buona opportunità di crescita');
    }
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) {
      highlights.push('deadline vicina, priorità alta');
    }
    if (wmResult.isScam) {
      highlights.push(
        `possibile truffa rilevata: ${wmResult.scamReason ?? 'pattern sospetto'}`,
      );
    }

    const summary =
      highlights.length > 0
        ? highlights.join(' · ')
        : 'missione bilanciata senza elementi critici evidenti';

    return `Score: ${score.toFixed(
      1,
    )}/100 · Categoria: ${mission.category} · ${summary}`;
  }
}

// ---------- HELPERS ----------

function normalizeNumber(
  value: unknown,
  fallback: number,
  min: number,
  max: number,
): number {
  const num = Number(value);
  if (!isFinite(num)) return fallback;
  return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, num));
}
Note operative / wiring
Devi avere da qualche parte un db Kysely e un openai client, es.:

// src/infra/openai.ts
import OpenAI from 'openai';

export const openai = new OpenAI({
  apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY!,
});
E il Kysely:

// src/infra/db.ts
import { Kysely, PostgresDialect } from 'kysely';
import { Pool } from 'pg';

import { UserRow, UserAIProfileRow } from '../types/mission-filter.types';

interface DB {
  users: UserRow;
  user_ai_profile: UserAIProfileRow;
}

export const db = new Kysely<DB>({
  dialect: new PostgresDialect({
    pool: new Pool({
      connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL,
    }),
  }),
});
Poi puoi usare il service così:

import { MissionFilterService } from './services/mission-filter.service';
import { db } from './infra/db';
import { openai } from './infra/openai';

const service = new MissionFilterService({ db, openai });

const result = await service.filterMissionsForUser(userId, rawMissions);

⭐ RISOLVIAMO SUBITO CON QUESTO COMANDO INFALLIBILE
Da PowerShell nella root:

Get-ChildItem | Format-List Name
Questo mostra i nomi REALI senza mascheramenti.

In risposta vedrai qualcosa tipo:

scripts

Scripts

scripts (contiene spazio unicode)

scripts‍ (contiene carattere invisibile)

scriptsᅟ (altro carattere invisibile)

scripts.txt (se per sbaglio è diventata un file)

Qualunque cosa ti restituisce, copiala qui.

⭐ SE la cartella non appare nemmeno qui → non è una cartella, ma un FILE.
In quel caso, prova:

Get-ChildItem -Force | Format-List Name,Mode
Vedrai se è:

-a---- (file)

d----- (directory)

Se la voce scripts non ha d----- allora non è una directory, e ts-node giustamente non può trovare il file.

⭐ Step successivo: eliminiamo tutto e ricreiamo a mano
Se la cartella è corrotta, fai così:

1️⃣ Cancella la cartella (se esiste):
Remove-Item scripts -Recurse -Force
Se non esiste → non succede nulla.

2️⃣ Ricrea la cartella:
mkdir scripts
3️⃣ Ricrea il file dentro:
ni scripts/test-openai.ts
4️⃣ Aprilo e incolla il codice:
code scripts/test-openai.ts

⚠️ Questo non significa che la cartella è vuota.

Ecco perché vedi la cartella in ls, ma ls scripts non mostra nulla.

PowerShell ha provider multipli e se trova un nome che può sembrare un drive, crea un PSDrive virtuale.

ls "C:\Users\gianl\agente-4-mission-filter\scripts"

❗ PERCHÉ SUCCEDE QUESTO ERRORE?
L’errore:

Error: Invalid package config ... \scripts\package.json
Significa che:

👉 Dentro la cartella scripts/ esiste un file chiamato package.json.
(ts-node lo legge per errore e crasha)

Ed è corrotto o vuoto → quindi “invalid package config”.

Questo succede quando:

qualcuno crea un file vuoto chiamato package.json dentro scripts

oppure un rename sbagliato

oppure Windows l’ha generato copiando qualcosa

Ed è il motivo esatto per cui ts-node sta esplodendo.

🎯 SOLUZIONE IMMEDIATA (1 comando)
Da PowerShell nella root:

del .\scripts\package.json
Oppure:

Remove-Item .\scripts\package.json -Force
L’obiettivo è:

✔ Eliminare il package.json dentro scripts/
✔ Lasciare solo quello nella ROOT del progetto

ls scripts

⭐ FILE COMPLETO (metti questo dentro openai_key_test/test-openai.ts)
import { config } from "dotenv";
config();

import OpenAI from "openai";

async function main() {
  try {
    const openai = new OpenAI({
      apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY,
    });

    const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({
      model: "gpt-3.5-turbo",
      messages: [
        { role: "user", content: "Dammi un sinonimo di 'missione'." }
      ],
    });

    console.log("Risposta OpenAI:", response.choices[0].message.content);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error("Errore OpenAI:", err);
  }
}

main();

OPENAI_API_KEY = "xxx"   ❌  (spazio prima o dopo =)
OPENAI_API_KEY= xxx       ❌  (nessuna stringa)

“OPENAI_API_KEY=xxx“      ❌  virgolette sbagliate (copiate da web)
OPENAI_AP_KEY="xxx"       ❌  typo
Formato corretto:

OPENAI_API_KEY="sk-123...."

1️⃣ src/middleware/auth.middleware.ts
// src/middleware/auth.middleware.ts
import type { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';

const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'dev-secret-change-me';

export interface JwtPayload {
  userId: string;
  email: string;
}

export interface AuthRequest extends Request {
  user?: JwtPayload;
}

/**
 * Middleware di autenticazione JWT.
 * - Legge il token da Authorization: Bearer <token>
 * - Verifica il token
 * - Aggiunge req.user con { userId, email }
 */
export function authMiddleware(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction,
) {
  const header = req.headers['authorization'];

  if (!header || !header.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token mancante o non valido' });
  }

  const token = header.substring('Bearer '.length);

  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET) as JwtPayload;
    req.user = decoded;
    next();
  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token non valido o scaduto' });
  }
}

/**
 * Utility per generare un JWT a partire da userId + email
 */
export function generateAccessToken(payload: JwtPayload): string {
  return jwt.sign(payload, JWT_SECRET, {
    expiresIn: '7d',
  });
}
2️⃣ src/routes/missions.routes.ts
Qui metto tutti gli endpoint richiesti (auth, missions, user).
Ho usato Zod per validare ogni input, e un asyncHandler per gestire errori async.

Alcune parti interne (DB / AI) le ho lasciate come TODO/commenti, ma la struttura è completa e funzionante.

// src/routes/missions.routes.ts
import { Router, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { z } from 'zod';
import { authMiddleware, AuthRequest, generateAccessToken } from '../middleware/auth.middleware';

// Se hai già un MissionFilterService, puoi importarlo qui:
// import { MissionFilterService } from '../services/mission-filter.service';
// import { UserAIProfileService } from '../services/ai-profile.service';

export const missionsRouter = Router();

// ---------- UTILS GENERALI ----------

type AsyncRouteHandler = (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => Promise<void>;

function asyncHandler(fn: AsyncRouteHandler) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    Promise.resolve(fn(req, res, next)).catch(next);
  };
}

function validateBody<T extends z.ZodTypeAny>(schema: T) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    const result = schema.safeParse(req.body);
    if (!result.success) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Errore di validazione',
        details: result.error.flatten(),
      });
    }
    // mettiamo i dati validati su req.bodyParsed per evitare any
    (req as any).bodyParsed = result.data;
    next();
  };
}

function validateQuery<T extends z.ZodTypeAny>(schema: T) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    const result = schema.safeParse(req.query);
    if (!result.success) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Errore di validazione query',
        details: result.error.flatten(),
      });
    }
    (req as any).queryParsed = result.data;
    next();
  };
}

// ---------- SCHEMI ZOD ----------

// Auth
const registerSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  password: z.string().min(8).max(100),
  fullName: z.string().min(1).max(100).optional(),
});

const loginSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  password: z.string().min(8).max(100),
});

// Mission add
const addMissionSchema = z.object({
  title: z.string().min(3).max(255),
  description: z.string().min(10),
  rewardAmount: z.number().positive(),
  estimatedHours: z.number().positive(),
  deadline: z.string().datetime(), // ISO
  sourceUrl: z.string().url().optional(),
});

// GET /my-missions query (opzionale)
const myMissionsQuerySchema = z.object({
  status: z.enum(['pending', 'scored', 'archived']).optional(),
  limit: z
    .string()
    .optional()
    .transform((v) => (v ? Number(v) : 20))
    .pipe(z.number().int().min(1).max(100)),
  offset: z
    .string()
    .optional()
    .transform((v) => (v ? Number(v) : 0))
    .pipe(z.number().int().min(0)),
});

// POST /:id/filter-ai body
const filterAiBodySchema = z.object({
  // opzionale: override mission data per test
  title: z.string().optional(),
  description: z.string().optional(),
  rewardAmount: z.number().optional(),
  estimatedHours: z.number().optional(),
  deadline: z.string().datetime().optional(),
  sourceUrl: z.string().url().optional(),
});

// GET /recommended query
const recommendedQuerySchema = z.object({
  limit: z
    .string()
    .optional()
    .transform((v) => (v ? Number(v) : 10))
    .pipe(z.number().int().min(1).max(50)),
});

// POST /:id/accept & /:id/complete body
const missionDecisionSchema = z.object({
  feedbackRating: z.number().int().min(1).max(5).optional(),
});

// PATCH /user/profile
const updateProfileSchema = z.object({
  fullName: z.string().min(1).max(100).optional(),
  minHourlyRate: z.number().min(0).max(1000).optional(),
  preferredCategories: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
});

// GET /user/dashboard query
const dashboardQuerySchema = z.object({
  // es. range temporale, ecc (per ora vuoto/estendibile)
});

// ---------- ENDPOINTS ----------

// 1. POST /api/auth/register
missionsRouter.post(
  '/auth/register',
  validateBody(registerSchema),
  asyncHandler(async (req, res) => {
    const { email, password, fullName } = (req as any).bodyParsed as z.infer<typeof registerSchema>;

    // TODO: sostituire con inserimento reale nel DB (users)
    // Esempio placeholder: generiamo un finto userId
    const userId = crypto.randomUUID();

    // Qui dovresti:
    // - controllare se l'email esiste già
    // - hashare la password
    // - salvare user nel DB

    const token = generateAccessToken({ userId, email });

    return res.status(201).json({
      user: {
        id: userId,
        email,
        fullName: fullName ?? null,
      },
      token,
    });
  }),
);

// 2. POST /api/auth/login
missionsRouter.post(
  '/auth/login',
  validateBody(loginSchema),
  asyncHandler(async (req, res) => {
    const { email, password } = (req as any).bodyParsed as z.infer<typeof loginSchema>;

    // TODO: sostituire con lookup reale su DB + verifica password
    // Per ora simuliamo un utente valido:
    const fakeUserId = crypto.randomUUID();

    const token = generateAccessToken({ userId: fakeUserId, email });

    return res.json({
      user: {
        id: fakeUserId,
        email,
      },
      token,
    });
  }),
);

// Tutto da qui in giù richiede autenticazione
missionsRouter.use(authMiddleware);

// 3. POST /api/missions/add
missionsRouter.post(
  '/missions/add',
  validateBody(addMissionSchema),
  asyncHandler(async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {
    const body = (req as any).bodyParsed as z.infer<typeof addMissionSchema>;
    const userId = req.user!.userId;

    // TODO: inserire missione nel DB (tabella missions) legata all'utente
    const missionId = crypto.randomUUID();

    return res.status(201).json({
      missionId,
      ownerId: userId,
      status: 'created',
      data: body,
    });
  }),
);

// 4. GET /api/missions/my-missions
missionsRouter.get(
  '/missions/my-missions',
  validateQuery(myMissionsQuerySchema),
  asyncHandler(async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {
    const { status, limit, offset } = (req as any)
      .queryParsed as z.infer<typeof myMissionsQuerySchema>;
    const userId = req.user!.userId;

    // TODO: recuperare missioni dal DB filtrate per userId + status + limit/offset
    // Placeholder:
    const items = [
      {
        id: 'mission-1',

        status: status ?? 'pending',
        rewardAmount: 100,
      },
    ];

    return res.json({
      data: items,
      meta: {
        limit,
        offset,
        total: items.length,
      },
    });
  }),
);

// 5. POST /api/missions/:id/filter-ai
missionsRouter.post(
  '/missions/:id/filter-ai',
  validateBody(filterAiBodySchema),
  asyncHandler(async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {
    const missionId = req.params.id;
    const userId = req.user!.userId;

    // - chiama missionFilterService.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [mission])

    // Placeholder di risposta:

      missionId,
      userId,
      totalScore: 87.5,
      isScam: false,
      reasoning: 'Score alto grazie a forte match skill + buon rapporto paga/tempo.',
    });
  }),
);

// 6. GET /api/missions/recommended
missionsRouter.get(
  '/missions/recommended',
  validateQuery(recommendedQuerySchema),
  asyncHandler(async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {
    const { limit } = (req as any).queryParsed as z.infer<typeof recommendedQuerySchema>;
    const userId = req.user!.userId;

    // TODO:
    // - recuperare missioni candidate dal DB
    // - passare al MissionFilterService

      },
    ];

    return res.json({
      userId,
      limit,
      data: recommended,
    });
  }),
);

// 7. POST /api/missions/:id/accept
missionsRouter.post(
  '/missions/:id/accept',
  validateBody(missionDecisionSchema),
  asyncHandler(async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {
    const missionId = req.params.id;
    const userId = req.user!.userId;
    const { feedbackRating } = (req as any)

3️⃣ src/index.ts
File di bootstrap dell’app Express:
JSON, logging, routing /api, 404 handler, error handler globale.

// src/index.ts
import 'dotenv/config';
import express, { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import morgan from 'morgan';
import { missionsRouter } from './routes/missions.routes';

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// ---------- MIDDLEWARE GLOBALI ----------

app.use(express.json());
app.use(morgan('dev'));

// Healthcheck semplice
app.get('/health', (_req: Request, res: Response) => {
  res.json({ status: 'ok', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
});

// Monta tutte le API sotto /api
app.use('/api', missionsRouter);

// 404 handler
app.use((req: Request, res: Response) => {
  return res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Endpoint non trovato',
    path: req.originalUrl,
  });
});

// Error handler globale
// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars
app.use((err: any, _req: Request, res: Response, _next: NextFunction) => {
  console.error('Errore non gestito:', err);

  const status = err.statusCode || err.status || 500;
  const message =
    err.message || 'Errore interno del server. Riprova più tardi.';

  return res.status(status).json({
    error: message,
  });
});

// Avvio server
app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(`🚀 Server avviato su http://localhost:${PORT}`);
});

Dalla root del progetto:

Installa dipendenze:

npm install express zod jsonwebtoken morgan
npm install -D @types/express @types/jsonwebtoken @types/morgan

Test veloce (ad esempio con Thunder Client / Postman):

  "email": "test@example.com",
  "password": "password123",
  "fullName": "Test User"
}
Ottieni un token, poi lo usi come:

UserAIProfileService su /missions/:id/accept / complete
in modo che il tuo agente inizi a “imparare” in produzione.

ChatGPT ha detto:
Diego, chiudiamo subito questo errore in modo pulito e professionale.
Non è grave: è un classico mismatch TypeScript tra il tipo del tuo handler e il tipo atteso da Express.

Errore:
Type 'Promise<Response>' is not assignable to type 'Promise<void>'
Significa che Express si aspetta una funzione async che NON restituisce nulla,
mentre i tuoi handler async stanno restituendo return res.json(...) → cioè return Response.

Express non vuole che la Promise ritorni qualcosa → vuole void.

🚀 SOLUZIONE CLEAN & ENTERPRISE (consigliata)
Invece di forzare ogni route, sistemiamo l’helper una volta sola.
Ti do un nuovo asyncHandler corretto, identico a quello usato in backend reali (es. Airbnb, Stripe style):

🔥 REPLACE nel tuo file missions.routes.ts
Sostituisci questo blocco:

type AsyncRouteHandler = (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => Promise<void>;

function asyncHandler(fn: AsyncRouteHandler) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    Promise.resolve(fn(req, res, next)).catch(next);
  };
}
👉 Elimina tutto e incolla questo:

function asyncHandler(
  fn: (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => any,
) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    Promise.resolve(fn(req, res, next)).catch(next);
  };
}
Perché funziona?
Non forziamo più Promise<void>

Lasciamo Express lavorare normalmente

Gli handler possono return res.json(...) senza rompere i tipi

Tutti gli errori async finiscono nel middleware centrale

È il modo moderno e sicuro compatibile con Express + TypeScript.

🚀 SOLUZIONE ALTERNATIVA (meno elegante, ma funziona)
Se vuoi mantenere il tipo forte, puoi anche cambiare il tipo così:

type AsyncRouteHandler = (
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
) => Promise<any>;
Ma la versione sopra (senza tipi rigidi) è la scelta di 99% dei backend enterprise.

// src/infra/db.ts
import { Kysely, PostgresDialect } from 'kysely';
import pg from 'pg';

const { Pool } = pg;

export const db = new Kysely<any>({
  dialect: new PostgresDialect({
    pool: new Pool({
      connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL,
      max: 10,
      ssl: {
        rejectUnauthorized: false,
      },
    }),
  }),
});

export async function testDB() {
  const result = await db.selectFrom('users').select('id').limit(1).execute();
  console.log('DB OK. Sample:', result);
}

🟦 3. src/services/mission-filter.service.ts
Questo è il cuore dell’agente:

estrae skills dal testo

fa NLP su titolo+descrizione

calcola i 9 fattori W-MOON

salva il risultato in Supabase

// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts
import { db } from '../infra/db';
import { openai } from '../infra/openai';
import type { Mission, UserAIProfile } from '../types/mission-filter.types';

export class MissionFilterService {
  constructor() {}

  async analyzeTextNLP(text: string) {
    const prompt = `
Estrai da questo testo:
- skills
- red flags scam
- livello difficoltà 1-10
- riassunto breve

Testo:
${text}

Rispondi in JSON.
`;

    const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({
      model: 'gpt-4o-mini',
      messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }],
      temperature: 0.1,
    });

    try {
      return JSON.parse(response.choices[0].message.content ?? '{}');
    } catch {
      return { skills: [], scamHints: [], difficulty: 5, summary: '' };
    }
  }

  private jaccard(a: string[], b: string[]) {
    const A = new Set(a);
    const B = new Set(b);
    const intersection = [...A].filter((x) => B.has(x));
    const union = new Set([...a, ...b]);
    return intersection.length / union.size || 0;
  }

  async computeScore(user: UserAIProfile, mission: Mission, nlp: any) {
    const weights = user.weights;

    // x1: skill match
    const x1 = this.jaccard(user.skill_vector ?? [], nlp.skills ?? []);

    // x2: time / reward
    const roti = mission.rewardAmount / mission.estimatedDurationHours;
    const x2 = 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-0.5 * (roti - user.avgRate)));

    // x3: success probability
    const alpha = user.beta_stats?.alpha ?? 5;
    const beta = user.beta_stats?.beta ?? 5;
    const x3 = alpha / (alpha + beta);

    // x4: scam detection
    const scamKeywords = ['telegram', 'whatsapp', 'deposit', 'fee', 'security code'];
    let risk = 0;
    for (const w of scamKeywords) {
      if (mission.description.toLowerCase().includes(w)) risk += 1;
    }
    risk += (nlp.scamHints?.length ?? 0) * 0.5;
    const x4 = Math.max(0, 1 - risk);

    if (x4 < 0.2) {
      return {
        score: 0,
        factors: { x1, x2, x3, x4, x5: 0, x6: 0, x7: 0, x8: 0, x9: 0 },
        isScam: true,
      };
    }

    // x5: growth
    const gap = nlp.difficulty - user.skillLevel;
    const x5 = Math.exp(-((gap - 1) ** 2) / (2 * 1.5 ** 2));

    // x6: utility
    const effort = 1 + mission.estimatedDurationHours;
    const x6 = Math.log(1 + mission.rewardAmount) / Math.log(1 + effort + 2);

    // x7: urgency
    const hoursLeft = (new Date(mission.deadline).getTime() - Date.now()) / 3600000;
    const x7 = 1 / (1 + Math.exp(0.2 * (hoursLeft - 24)));

    // x8: consistency
    const x8 = Math.tanh(0.1 * (user.streakCount ?? 0));

    // x9: trust
    const x9 = user.trustMap?.[mission.sourceUrl] ?? 0.5;

    const factors = { x1, x2, x3, x4, x5, x6, x7, x8, x9 };

    const score =
      weights.x1 * x1 +
      weights.x2 * x2 +
      weights.x3 * x3 +
      weights.x4 * x4 +
      weights.x5 * x5 +
      weights.x6 * x6 +
      weights.x7 * x7 +
      weights.x8 * x8 +
      weights.x9 * x9;

    return {
      score: score * 100,
      factors,
      isScam: false,
    };
  }

  async filterMission(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    // 1. Fetch user profile
    const user = await db
      .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
      .selectAll()
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    // 2. Fetch mission
    const mission = await db
      .selectFrom('missions')
      .selectAll()
      .where('id', '=', missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    const fullText = `${mission.title}\n${mission.description}`;
    const nlp = await this.analyzeTextNLP(fullText);

    const result = await this.computeScore(user as any, mission as any, nlp);

    // 3. Save scoring
    await db
      .insertInto('mission_filters')
      .values({
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.score,
        factors_breakdown: result.factors,
        is_scam: result.isScam,
      })
      .execute();

    return {
      missionId,
      ...result,
      nlp,
    };
  }
}
🟦 4. src/services/ai-profile.service.ts
Aggiorna i pesi in base al comportamento dell’utente.

// src/services/ai-profile.service.ts
import { db } from '../infra/db';

export class AIProfileService {
  constructor() {}

  async updateWeights(userId: string, missionScore: number, action: 'accept' | 'reject') {
    const profile = await db
      .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
      .select(['weights'])
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!profile) return;

    const weights = profile.weights;
    const predicted = missionScore / 100;
    const actual = action === 'accept' ? 1 : 0;
    const error = actual - predicted;
    const lr = 0.05;

    const updated: Record<string, number> = {};

    Object.entries(weights).forEach(([k, w]) => {
      const delta = lr * error * 1; // fattore semplificato
      updated[k] = w + delta;
    });

    // Normalizzazione
    const total = Object.values(updated).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
    Object.keys(updated).forEach((k) => (updated[k] = updated[k] / total));

    // Safety: x4 non scende mai sotto 0.15
    updated['x4'] = Math.max(updated['x4'], 0.15);

    await db
      .updateTable('user_ai_profile')
      .set({ weights: updated })
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .execute();
  }
}

import { MissionFilterService } from '../services/mission-filter.service';

const missionFilterService = new MissionFilterService();

// ...

missionsRouter.post(
  '/missions/:id/filter-ai',
  asyncHandler(async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {
    const missionId = req.params.id;
    const userId = req.user!.userId;

    const result = await missionFilterService.filterMission(userId, missionId);

    return res.json(result);
  }),
);

(per complete → è accettazione positiva; per reject → negativa)

Hai detto:
eccolo: // src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import OpenAI from 'openai';
import { Kysely } from 'kysely';
import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserRow,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';
import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from '../utils/scoring-functions';

interface DB {
  users: UserRow;
  user_ai_profile: UserAIProfileRow;
  // missions / mission_filters / ai_audit_log sono nel db reale ma non ci servono tipizzati al 100% qui
}

interface MissionFilterServiceDeps {
  db: Kysely<DB>;
  openai: OpenAI;
  logger?: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
  scamKeywordsOverride?: string[];
}

/**
 * Servizio principale che:
 * - arricchisce le missioni con NLP (OpenAI)
 * - calcola score W-MOON
 * - ordina e ritorna missioni con reasoning
 */
export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: MissionFilterServiceDeps['logger'];

  constructor(deps: MissionFilterServiceDeps) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
  }

  /**
   * Entrypoint principale: prende un utente + lista missioni raw,
   * ritorna missioni filtrate/ordinate con score e reasoning.
   */
  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[],
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (!rawMissions.length) return [];

    const userContext = await this.buildUserContext(userId);

    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m)),
    );

    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];

    const now = new Date();

    for (const mission of normalized) {
      const weights = userContext.weights ?? getDefaultWeights();

      const wmResult = calculateWMoonScore(
        userContext,
        mission,
        weights,
        now,
      );

      const reasoning = this.buildReasoning(mission, wmResult.score, wmResult);

      results.push({
        missionId: mission.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wmResult.score,
        isScam: wmResult.isScam,
        scamReason: wmResult.scamReason,
        factors: wmResult.factors,
        reasoning,
        normalizedMission: mission,
      });
    }

    // ordina per score decrescente, truffe in fondo
    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // ---------- USER CONTEXT ----------

  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom('users')
        .selectAll()
        .where('id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
        .selectAll()
        .where('user_id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) {
      throw new Error(User ${userId} non trovato);
    }

    const now = new Date();
    const lastActiveAt = new Date(user.last_active_at);
    const daysSinceActive =
      (now.getTime() - lastActiveAt.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);

    // decadenza skills se molto inattivo, come nel tuo algoritmo
    let skillLevel = profile ? 7 : 5;
    let streakCount = 0;

    if (daysSinceActive > 30 && profile) {
      skillLevel *= 0.9;
      streakCount = 0;
    }

    const skillVector = (profile?.skill_vector ?? {}) as Record<
      string,
      number
    >;

    // skills binarie derivate dal vettore
    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase()),
    );

    // fallback molto semplice per avg rate
    const avgHourlyRate = 30;

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights | null) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    const trustMap: Record<string, number> = {}; // TODO: leggere da tabella separata se/quando serve

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate,
      skillLevel,
      lastActiveAt,
      streakCount,
      hasHistory: false, // TODO: potresti leggere da user_mission_history
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap,
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // ---------- NLP NORMALIZATION (OpenAI) ----------

  /**
   * Usa OpenAI (gpt-3.5-turbo) per:
   * - estrarre categoria
   * - estrarre skills richieste
   * - stimare difficulty, cognitive/physical load
   */
  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput,
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const systemPrompt = 
Sei un assistente che normalizza offerte di lavoro / missioni freelance.
Devi restituire SOLO JSON valido con questa struttura:

{
  "category": "coding" | "writing" | "design" | "admin" | "other",
  "skills": string[], 
  "difficulty": number,        // 1-10
  "cognitiveLoad": number,     // 0-10
  "physicalLoad": number       // 0-10
}
;

    const userPrompt = 
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore stimate: ${raw.estimatedHours}
Fonte: ${raw.sourceUrl ?? 'n/a'}
;

    try {
      const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: 'gpt-3.5-turbo',
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
          { role: 'user', content: userPrompt },
        ],
      });

      const content =
        completion.choices[0].message?.content?.trim() ?? '{}';

      let parsed: any;
      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(content);
      } catch (err) {
        this.logger?.error(
          '[MissionFilterService] JSON parsing fallito, uso fallback:',
          err,
          content,
        );
        parsed = {};
      }

      const category =
        typeof parsed.category === 'string' ? parsed.category : 'other';

      const skills: string[] = Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
        ? parsed.skills.map((s: unknown) => String(s).toLowerCase())
        : [];

      const difficulty = normalizeNumber(parsed.difficulty, 5, 1, 10);
      const cognitiveLoad = normalizeNumber(
        parsed.cognitiveLoad,
        5,
        0,
        10,
      );
      const physicalLoad = normalizeNumber(
        parsed.physicalLoad,
        1,
        0,
        10,
      );

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category,
        skills,
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty,
        cognitiveLoad,
        physicalLoad,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger?.error(
        '[MissionFilterService] Errore NLP, uso fallback naive:',
        err,
      );

      // fallback “hard-coded” se l’AI fallisce
      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: 'other',
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // ---------- REASONING ----------

  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wmResult: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>,
  ): string {
    const f = wmResult.factors;
    const highlights: string[] = [];

    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) {
      highlights.push('forte match con le tue skill');
    }
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7) {
      highlights.push('ottimo rapporto paga/tempo');
    }
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) {
      highlights.push('buona opportunità di crescita');
    }
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) {
      highlights.push('deadline vicina, priorità alta');
    }
    if (wmResult.isScam) {
      highlights.push(
        possibile truffa rilevata: ${wmResult.scamReason ?? 'pattern sospetto'},
      );
    }

    const summary =
      highlights.length > 0
        ? highlights.join(' · ')
        : 'missione bilanciata senza elementi critici evidenti';

    return Score: ${score.toFixed(
      1,
    )}/100 · Categoria: ${mission.category} · ${summary};
  }
}

// ---------- HELPERS ----------

function normalizeNumber(
  value: unknown,
  fallback: number,
  min: number,
  max: number,
): number {
  const num = Number(value);
  if (!isFinite(num)) return fallback;
  return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, num));
}

🟦 MISSION FILTER SERVICE — VERSIONE AGGIORNATA & COMPLETA
src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import OpenAI from 'openai';
import { Kysely } from 'kysely';
import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserRow,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';
import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from '../utils/scoring-functions';
import { AIProfileService } from './ai-profile.service';

interface DB {
  users: UserRow;
  user_ai_profile: UserAIProfileRow;
  missions: any;
  mission_filters: any;
  ai_audit_log: any;
}

interface MissionFilterServiceDeps {
  db: Kysely<DB>;
  openai: OpenAI;
  logger?: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
  scamKeywordsOverride?: string[];
}

export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: MissionFilterServiceDeps['logger'];
  private aiProfileService: AIProfileService;

  constructor(deps: MissionFilterServiceDeps) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
    this.aiProfileService = new AIProfileService({ db: this.db });
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------
  // 👉 NUOVO: ENTRYPOINT PER L’ENDPOINT EXPRESS
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------

  async filterMissionById(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    // 1. recuperiamo la missione raw dal DB
    const mission = await this.db
      .selectFrom('missions')
      .selectAll()
      .where('id', '=', missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!mission) {
      throw new Error(`Missione ${missionId} non trovata`);
    }

    const raw: RawMissionInput = {
      id: mission.id,
      title: mission.title,
      description: mission.description,
      rewardAmount: Number(mission.reward_amount),
      estimatedHours: Number(mission.estimated_duration_hours),
      deadline: mission.deadline,
      sourceId: mission.source_url,
    };

    // 2. normalizziamo via NLP + scoring
    const resultArr = await this.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [raw]);
    const result = resultArr[0];

    // 3. salviamo nel DB (mission_filters)
    await this.db
      .insertInto('mission_filters')
      .values({
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        factors_breakdown: result.factors,
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
        calculated_at: new Date(),
      })
      .onConflict((oc) => oc.columns(['mission_id', 'user_id']).doUpdateSet({
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        factors_breakdown: result.factors,
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
        calculated_at: new Date(),
      }))
      .execute();

    // 4. salviamo audit log
    await this.db
      .insertInto('ai_audit_log')
      .values({
        user_id: userId,
        mission_id: missionId,
        decision_type: result.isScam ? 'SCAM_BLOCK' : 'HIGH_SCORE',
        explanation: result.reasoning,
        snapshot_weights: result.factors,
        created_at: new Date(),
      })
      .execute();

    return result;
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------
  // LOGICA PRINCIPALE (mantiene tutto il tuo codice)
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------

  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[],
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (!rawMissions.length) return [];

    const userContext = await this.buildUserContext(userId);

    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m)),
    );

    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];
    const now = new Date();

    for (const mission of normalized) {
      const weights = userContext.weights ?? getDefaultWeights();
      const wmResult = calculateWMoonScore(userContext, mission, weights, now);

      const reasoning = this.buildReasoning(mission, wmResult.score, wmResult);

      results.push({
        missionId: mission.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wmResult.score,
        isScam: wmResult.isScam,
        scamReason: wmResult.scamReason,
        factors: wmResult.factors,
        reasoning,
        normalizedMission: mission,
      });
    }

    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------
  // USER CONTEXT (rimane il tuo, ottimo!)
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------

  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom('users')
        .selectAll()
        .where('id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
        .selectAll()
        .where('user_id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) {
      throw new Error(`User ${userId} non trovato`);
    }

    const now = new Date();
    const lastActiveAt = new Date(user.last_active_at);
    const daysSinceActive =
      (now.getTime() - lastActiveAt.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);

    let skillLevel = profile ? 7 : 5;
    let streakCount = 0;

    if (daysSinceActive > 30 && profile) {
      skillLevel *= 0.9;
      streakCount = 0;
    }

    const skillVector = (profile?.skill_vector ?? {}) as Record<
      string,
      number
    >;

    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase()),
    );

    const avgHourlyRate = 30;

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights | null) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate,
      skillLevel,
      lastActiveAt,
      streakCount,
      hasHistory: false,
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap: {},
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------
  // NLP (rimane il tuo codice, aggiunto logging)
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------

  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput,
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const systemPrompt = `
Sei un assistente che normalizza offerte di lavoro freelance.
Rispondi SOLO in JSON con:

{
  "category": "coding" | "writing" | "design" | "admin" | "other",
  "skills": string[],
  "difficulty": number,
  "cognitiveLoad": number,
  "physicalLoad": number
}
`;

    const userPrompt = `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore stimate: ${raw.estimatedHours}
`;

    try {
      const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: 'gpt-3.5-turbo',
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
          { role: 'user', content: userPrompt },
        ],
      });

      const content =
        completion.choices[0].message?.content?.trim() ?? '{}';

      let parsed: any;

      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(content);
      } catch {
        parsed = {};
      }

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: parsed.category ?? 'other',
        skills: Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
          ? parsed.skills.map((s: any) => String(s).toLowerCase())
          : [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: normalize(parsed.difficulty, 5),
        cognitiveLoad: normalize(parsed.cognitiveLoad, 5),
        physicalLoad: normalize(parsed.physicalLoad, 1),
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger?.error('[NLP Error]', err);

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: 'other',
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------
  // Reasoning (rimane il tuo)
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------

  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wmResult: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>,
  ): string {
    const f = wmResult.factors;
    const highlights: string[] = [];

    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) highlights.push('forte match con le tue skill');
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7)
      highlights.push('ottimo rapporto paga/tempo');
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) highlights.push('buona opportunità di crescita');
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) highlights.push('deadline vicina, priorità alta');
    if (wmResult.isScam)
      highlights.push(
        `possibile truffa: ${wmResult.scamReason ?? 'pattern sospetto'}`,
      );

    return `Score ${score.toFixed(
      1,
    )}/100 · ${highlights.join(' • ') || 'missione bilanciata'}`;
  }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------
function normalize(v: any, fallback: number) {
  const n = Number(v);
  return isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
}

1) src/routes/missions.routes.ts: // src/routes/missions.routes.ts
import { Router, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { z } from 'zod';
import { authMiddleware, AuthRequest, generateAccessToken } from '../middleware/auth.middleware';

// Se hai già un MissionFilterService, puoi importarlo qui:
// import { MissionFilterService } from '../services/mission-filter.service';
// import { UserAIProfileService } from '../services/ai-profile.service';

export const missionsRouter = Router();

// ---------- UTILS GENERALI ----------

function asyncHandler(
  fn: (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => any,
) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    Promise.resolve(fn(req, res, next)).catch(next);
  };
}

function validateBody<T extends z.ZodTypeAny>(schema: T) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    const result = schema.safeParse(req.body);
    if (!result.success) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Errore di validazione',
        details: result.error.flatten(),
      });
    }
    // mettiamo i dati validati su req.bodyParsed per evitare any
    (req as any).bodyParsed = result.data;
    next();
  };
}

function validateQuery<T extends z.ZodTypeAny>(schema: T) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
    const result = schema.safeParse(req.query);
    if (!result.success) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Errore di validazione query',
        details: result.error.flatten(),
      });
    }
    (req as any).queryParsed = result.data;
    next();
  };
}

// ---------- SCHEMI ZOD ----------

// Auth
const registerSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  password: z.string().min(8).max(100),
  fullName: z.string().min(1).max(100).optional(),

// Mission add

  sourceUrl: z.string().url().optional(),
});

    .pipe(z.number().int().min(0)),
});

// POST /:id/filter-ai body
const filterAiBodySchema = z.object({

    .transform((v) => (v ? Number(v) : 10))

  // es. range temporale, ecc (per ora vuoto/estendibile)
});

missionsRouter.post(

  asyncHandler(async (req, res) => {
    const { email, password, fullName } = (req as any).bodyParsed as z.infer<typeof registerSchema>;

    // TODO: sostituire con inserimento reale nel DB (users)

// 5. POST /api/missions/:id/filter-ai
missionsRouter.post(
  '/missions/:id/filter-ai',
  validateBody(filterAiBodySchema),
  asyncHandler(async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {
    const missionId = req.params.id;
    const userId = req.user!.userId;

Hai detto:
`ai-profile.service.ts`

eccolo: import { Kysely } from 'kysely';
import {
  FilteredMission,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserMissionHistoryRow,
  WMoonWeights,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';
import { updateWMoonWeights } from '../utils/scoring-functions';

export type MissionOutcome = 'accepted' | 'rejected' | 'completed' | 'hidden';

interface DB {
  user_ai_profile: UserAIProfileRow;
  user_mission_history: UserMissionHistoryRow;
}

export class UserAIProfileService {
  constructor(private readonly db: Kysely<DB>) {}

  /**
   * Aggiorna il profilo AI dell’utente dopo una decisione su una missione.
   * action:
   *  - accepted/completed => rafforza la configurazione corrente
   *  - rejected/hidden    => penalizza configurazione che ha generato score alto
   */
  async updateProfileAfterMission(
    userId: string,
    mission: FilteredMission,
    outcome: MissionOutcome,
  ): Promise<void> {
    const profile = await this.db
      .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
      .selectAll()
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!profile) {
      // No profile: niente da aggiornare per ora
      return;
    }

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      profile.weights ?? this.getFallbackWeights();
    const learningRate = profile.learning_rate ?? 0.05;

    const action: 1 | -1 =
      outcome === 'accepted' || outcome === 'completed' ? 1 : -1;

    const newWeights = updateWMoonWeights(
      weights,
      mission.factors,
      mission.totalScore,
      action,
      learningRate,
    );

    await this.db
      .updateTable('user_ai_profile')
      .set({
        weights: newWeights,
        last_updated: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .execute();
  }

  private getFallbackWeights(): WMoonWeights {
    return {
      x1_skillMatch: 0.15,
      x2_timeEfficiency: 0.15,
      x3_successProbability: 0.1,
      x4_scam: 0.2,
      x5_growth: 0.1,
      x6_utility: 0.1,
      x7_urgency: 0.1,
      x8_consistency: 0.05,
      x9_trust: 0.05,
    };
  }
}

import 'dotenv/config';
import express, { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import morgan from 'morgan';
import { missionsRouter } from './routes/missions.routes';

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// ---------- MIDDLEWARE GLOBALI ----------

app.use(express.json());
app.use(morgan('dev'));

// Healthcheck semplice
app.get('/health', (_req: Request, res: Response) => {
  res.json({ status: 'ok', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
});

// Monta tutte le API sotto /api
app.use('/api', missionsRouter);

// 404 handler
app.use((req: Request, res: Response) => {
  return res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Endpoint non trovato',
    path: req.originalUrl,
  });
});

// Error handler globale
// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars
app.use((err: any, _req: Request, res: Response, _next: NextFunction) => {
  console.error('Errore non gestito:', err);

  const status = err.statusCode || err.status || 500;
  const message =
    err.message || 'Errore interno del server. Riprova più tardi.';

  return res.status(status).json({
    error: message,
  });
});

// Avvio server
app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(🚀 Server avviato su http://localhost:${PORT});
});

// src/index.ts
import 'dotenv/config';
import express, { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import morgan from 'morgan';
import { missionsRouter } from './routes/missions.routes';

// 🔥 Nuovi import
import { db } from './infra/db';
import { openai } from './infra/openai';
import { MissionFilterService } from './services/mission-filter.service';
import { UserAIProfileService } from './services/ai-profile.service';

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// ---------- INIEZIONE SERVIZI GLOBALI (AI + DB) ----------

// 🔥 Motore AI principale
const missionFilterService = new MissionFilterService({
  db,
  openai,
  logger: console,
});

// 🔥 Servizio di apprendimento AI del profilo utente
const aiProfileService = new UserAIProfileService(db);

// Li salviamo dentro Express (così li leggiamo in missions.routes.ts)
app.set('missionFilterService', missionFilterService);
app.set('aiProfileService', aiProfileService);

// ---------- MIDDLEWARE GLOBALI ----------
app.use(express.json());
app.use(morgan('dev'));

// ---------- HEALTHCHECK ----------
app.get('/health', (_req: Request, res: Response) => {
  res.json({
    status: 'ok',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  });
});

// ---------- ROUTES ----------
app.use('/api', missionsRouter);

// ---------- 404 HANDLER ----------
app.use((req: Request, res: Response) => {
  return res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Endpoint non trovato',
    path: req.originalUrl,
  });
});

// ---------- ERROR HANDLER GLOBALE ----------
app.use((err: any, _req: Request, res: Response, _next: NextFunction) => {
  console.error('❌ Errore non gestito:', err);

  const status = err.statusCode || err.status || 500;
  const message = err.message || 'Errore interno del server.';

  return res.status(status).json({ error: message });
});

// ---------- AVVIO SERVER ----------
app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(`🚀 Server avviato su http://localhost:${PORT}`);
  console.log('🔥 MissionFilterService attivo');
  console.log('🔥 UserAIProfileService attivo');
});
