📁 src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import OpenAI from 'openai';
import { Kysely } from 'kysely';

import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';

import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from '../utils/scoring-functions';

import { UserAIProfileService } from './ai-profile.service';
import { DB } from '../types/db';

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// SERVICE
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
  private aiProfileService: UserAIProfileService;

  constructor(deps: {
    db: Kysely<DB>;
    openai: OpenAI;
    logger?: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
    scamKeywordsOverride?: string[];
  }) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
    this.aiProfileService = new UserAIProfileService(this.db);
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🚀 ENTRYPOINT: /missions/:id/filter-ai
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  async filterMissionById(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    const mission = await this.db
      .selectFrom('missions')
      .selectAll()
      .where('id', '=', missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!mission) {
      throw new Error(`Mission ${missionId} non trovata`);
    }

    const raw: RawMissionInput = {
      id: mission.id,
      title: mission.title,
      description: mission.description ?? '',
      rewardAmount: Number(mission.reward_amount ?? 0),
      estimatedHours: Number(mission.estimated_duration_hours ?? 0),
      deadline: mission.deadline ? new Date(mission.deadline) : new Date(),
      sourceId: mission.source_url ?? '',
    };

    const results = await this.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [raw]);
    const result = results[0];

    // Salva scoring
    await this.db
      .insertInto('mission_filters')
      .values({
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        factors_breakdown: result.factors,
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
        calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .onConflict((oc) =>
        oc.columns(['mission_id', 'user_id']).doUpdateSet({
          total_score: result.totalScore,
          factors_breakdown: result.factors,
          is_scam: result.isScam,
          scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
          calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        }),
      )
      .execute();

    // Audit log
    await this.db
      .insertInto('ai_audit_log')
      .values({
        user_id: userId,
        mission_id: missionId,
        decision_type: result.isScam ? 'SCAM_BLOCK' : 'HIGH_SCORE',
        explanation: result.reasoning,
        snapshot_weights: result.factors,
        created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .execute();

    return result;
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // MAIN FILTER
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[],
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (!rawMissions.length) return [];

    const userContext = await this.buildUserContext(userId);
    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m)),
    );

    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];
    const now = new Date();

    for (const m of normalized) {
      const weights = userContext.weights ?? getDefaultWeights();
      const wmResult = calculateWMoonScore(userContext, m, weights, now);

      const reasoning = this.buildReasoning(m, wmResult.score, wmResult);

      results.push({
        missionId: m.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wmResult.score,
        isScam: wmResult.isScam,
        scamReason: wmResult.scamReason,
        factors: wmResult.factors,
        reasoning,
        normalizedMission: m,
      });
    }

    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // USER CONTEXT
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db.selectFrom('users').selectAll().where('id', '=', userId).executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
        .selectAll()
        .where('user_id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) throw new Error(`User ${userId} non trovato`);

    const now = new Date();
    const lastActive = new Date(user.last_active_at);
    const daysInactive = (now.getTime() - lastActive.getTime()) / 86400000;

    let skillLevel = profile ? 7 : 5;
    let streakCount = 0;

    if (daysInactive > 30 && profile) {
      skillLevel *= 0.9;
      streakCount = 0;
    }

    const skillVector = profile?.skill_vector ?? {};
    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, lvl]) => lvl > 0.3)
        .map(([name]) => name.toLowerCase()),
    );

    const weights: WMoonWeights = (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate: 30,
      skillLevel,
      lastActiveAt: lastActive,
      streakCount,
      hasHistory: false,
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap: {},
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // NLP NORMALIZATION
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(raw: RawMissionInput): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const sysPrompt = `
Sei un assistente che normalizza offerte freelance.
Rispondi SOLO JSON:

{
  "category": "coding" | "writing" | "design" | "admin" | "other",
  "skills": string[],
  "difficulty": number,
  "cognitiveLoad": number,
  "physicalLoad": number
}
`;

    const userPrompt = `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore: ${raw.estimatedHours}
`;

    try {
      const out = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: 'gpt-3.5-turbo',
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: sysPrompt },
          { role: 'user', content: userPrompt },
        ],
      });

      const txt = out.choices[0].message?.content?.trim() ?? '{}';
      let parsed: any;

      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(txt);
      } catch {
        parsed = {};
      }

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: parsed.category ?? 'other',
        skills: Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
          ? parsed.skills.map((s: any) => String(s).toLowerCase())
          : [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: normalizeNum(parsed.difficulty, 5),
        cognitiveLoad: normalizeNum(parsed.cognitiveLoad, 5),
        physicalLoad: normalizeNum(parsed.physicalLoad, 1),
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: 'other',
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // REASONING
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wmResult: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>,
  ): string {
    const f = wmResult.factors;
    const parts: string[] = [];

    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) parts.push('forte match skill');
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7) parts.push('ottimo rapporto paga/tempo');
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) parts.push('opportunità di crescita');
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) parts.push('alta urgenza');
    if (wmResult.isScam) parts.push(`possibile truffa: ${wmResult.scamReason}`);

    return `Score ${score.toFixed(1)}/100 • ${parts.join(' • ') || 'bilanciata'}`;
  }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// HELPERS
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

function normalizeNum(v: any, fallback: number): number {
  const n = Number(v);
  return isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
}

import 'dotenv/config';
import express, { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import morgan from 'morgan';
import { missionsRouter } from './routes/missions.routes';
import { db } from './infra/db';

  db,

app.use((req: Request, res: Response) => {

    path: req.originalUrl,

});

  console.error('Errore non gestito:', err);

  const status = err.statusCode || err.status || 500;
  const message =
    err.message || 'Errore interno del server. Riprova più tardi.';

  return res.status(status).json({
    error: message,
  });
});

});

✅ PASTE COMPLETO DI src/services/mission-filter.service.ts
// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import OpenAI from 'openai';
import { Kysely } from 'kysely';

import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';

import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from '../utils/scoring-functions';

import { UserAIProfileService } from './ai-profile.service';
import { DB } from '../types/db';

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// SERVICE PRINCIPALE
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
  private aiProfileService: UserAIProfileService;

  constructor(deps: {
    db: Kysely<DB>;
    openai: OpenAI;
    logger?: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
  }) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
    this.aiProfileService = new UserAIProfileService(this.db);
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🚀 ENTRYPOINT PRINCIPALE
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  async filterMissionById(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    const mission = await this.db
      .selectFrom('missions')
      .selectAll()
      .where('id', '=', missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!mission) {
      throw new Error(`Mission ${missionId} non trovata`);
    }

    const raw: RawMissionInput = {
      id: mission.id,
      title: mission.title,
      description: mission.description ?? '',
      rewardAmount: Number(mission.reward_amount ?? 0),
      estimatedHours: Number(mission.estimated_duration_hours ?? 0),
      deadline: mission.deadline ? new Date(mission.deadline) : new Date(),
      sourceId: mission.source_url ?? '',
    };

    const results = await this.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [raw]);
    const result = results[0];

    await this.db
      .insertInto('mission_filters')
      .values({
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        factors_breakdown: result.factors,
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
        calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .onConflict((oc) =>
        oc.columns(['mission_id', 'user_id']).doUpdateSet({
          total_score: result.totalScore,
          factors_breakdown: result.factors,
          is_scam: result.isScam,
          scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
          calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        }),
      )
      .execute();

    await this.db
      .insertInto('ai_audit_log')
      .values({
        user_id: userId,
        mission_id: missionId,
        decision_type: result.isScam ? 'SCAM_BLOCK' : 'HIGH_SCORE',
        explanation: result.reasoning,
        snapshot_weights: result.factors,
        created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .execute();

    return result;
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🌕 LOGICA W-MOON
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[],
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (!rawMissions.length) return [];

    const userContext = await this.buildUserContext(userId);

    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m)),
    );

    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];
    const now = new Date();

    for (const mission of normalized) {
      const weights = userContext.weights ?? getDefaultWeights();

      const wmResult = calculateWMoonScore(
        userContext,
        mission,
        weights,
        now,
      );

      const reasoning = this.buildReasoning(mission, wmResult.score, wmResult);

      results.push({
        missionId: mission.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wmResult.score,
        isScam: wmResult.isScam,
        scamReason: wmResult.scamReason,
        factors: wmResult.factors,
        reasoning,
        normalizedMission: mission,
      });
    }

    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 👤 USER CONTEXT
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom('users')
        .selectAll()
        .where('id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
        .selectAll()
        .where('user_id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) throw new Error(`User ${userId} non trovato`);

    const now = new Date();
    const lastActiveAt = new Date(user.last_active_at);
    const daysSince = (now.getTime() - lastActiveAt.getTime()) / 86400000;

    let skillLevel = profile ? 7 : 5;
    let streakCount = 0;

    if (daysSince > 30 && profile) {
      skillLevel *= 0.9;
      streakCount = 0;
    }

    const skillVector = profile?.skill_vector ?? {};
    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase()),
    );

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate: 30,
      skillLevel,
      lastActiveAt,
      streakCount,
      hasHistory: false,
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap: {},
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🤖 NLP NORMALIZATION
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput,
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const systemPrompt = `
Sei un assistente che normalizza missioni freelance.
Rispondi SOLO JSON:

{
  "category": "coding" | "writing" | "design" | "admin" | "other",
  "skills": string[],
  "difficulty": number,
  "cognitiveLoad": number,
  "physicalLoad": number
}
`.trim();

    const userPrompt = `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore: ${raw.estimatedHours}
`.trim();

    try {
      const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: 'gpt-3.5-turbo',
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
          { role: 'user', content: userPrompt },
        ],
      });

      const content = completion.choices[0].message?.content?.trim() ?? '{}';

      let parsed: any;
      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(content);
      } catch {
        parsed = {};
      }

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: parsed.category ?? 'other',
        skills: Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
          ? parsed.skills.map((s) => String(s).toLowerCase())
          : [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: normalize(parsed.difficulty, 5),
        cognitiveLoad: normalize(parsed.cognitiveLoad, 5),
        physicalLoad: normalize(parsed.physicalLoad, 1),
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger.error('[NLP ERROR]', err);

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: 'other',
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🧠 REASONING
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wmResult: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>,
  ): string {
    const f = wmResult.factors;
    const h: string[] = [];

    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) h.push('forte match skill');
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7) h.push('ottimo rapporto paga/tempo');
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) h.push('opportunità di crescita');
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) h.push('alta urgenza');
    if (wmResult.isScam) h.push(`possibile truffa: ${wmResult.scamReason}`);

    return `Score ${score.toFixed(1)}/100 • ${h.join(' • ') || 'bilanciata'}`;
  }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
function normalize(v: any, fallback: number) {
  const n = Number(v);
  return isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
}

// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import OpenAI from "openai";
import { Kysely } from "kysely";

import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserRow,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
  WMoonFactorKey
} from "../types/mission-filter.types";

import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights
} from "../utils/scoring-functions";

import { UserAIProfileService } from "./ai-profile.service";
import { DB } from "../types/db";

export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: any;
  private aiProfileService: UserAIProfileService;

  constructor(deps: { db: Kysely<DB>; openai: OpenAI; logger?: any }) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
    this.aiProfileService = new UserAIProfileService(this.db);
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FILTRO SINGOLA MISSIONE VIA ID
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  async filterMissionById(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    const mission = await this.db
      .selectFrom("missions")
      .selectAll()
      .where("id", "=", missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!mission) throw new Error(`Mission ${missionId} non trovata.`);

    const raw: RawMissionInput = {
      id: mission.id,
      title: mission.title,
      description: mission.description ?? "",
      rewardAmount: Number(mission.reward_amount),
      estimatedHours: Number(mission.estimated_duration_hours),
      deadline: new Date(mission.deadline),
      sourceId: mission.source_url ?? ""
    };

    const [result] = await this.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [raw]);

    // Salva scoring
    await this.db
      .insertInto("mission_filters")
      .values({
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
        calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        factors_breakdown: JSON.stringify(result.factors)
      })
      .onConflict((oc) =>
        oc.columns(["mission_id", "user_id"]).doUpdateSet({
          total_score: result.totalScore,
          is_scam: result.isScam,
          scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
          calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
          factors_breakdown: JSON.stringify(result.factors)
        })
      )
      .execute();

    // Salva audit log
    await this.db
      .insertInto("ai_audit_log")
      .values({
        user_id: userId,
        mission_id: missionId,
        decision_type: result.isScam ? "SCAM_BLOCK" : "HIGH_SCORE",
        explanation: result.reasoning,
        snapshot_weights: JSON.stringify(result.factors),
        created_at: new Date().toISOString()
      })
      .execute();

    return result;
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FILTRO MULTIPLE
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[]
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (rawMissions.length === 0) return [];

    const userCtx = await this.buildUserContext(userId);
    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m))
    );

    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];
    const now = new Date();

    for (const mission of normalized) {
      const wm = calculateWMoonScore(userCtx, mission, userCtx.weights, now);

      results.push({
        missionId: mission.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wm.score,
        isScam: wm.isScam,
        scamReason: wm.scamReason,
        factors: wm.factors,
        reasoning: this.buildReasoning(mission, wm.score, wm),
        normalizedMission: mission
      });
    }

    return results.sort((a, b) => b.totalScore - a.totalScore);
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // USER CONTEXT
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom("users")
        .selectAll()
        .where("id", "=", userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom("user_ai_profile")
        .selectAll()
        .where("user_id", "=", userId)
        .executeTakeFirst()
    ]);

    if (!user) throw new Error(`User ${userId} not found`);

    const skillVector = (profile?.skill_vector ?? {}) as Record<string, number>;

    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase())
    );

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate: 30,
      skillLevel: 5,
      lastActiveAt: new Date(user.last_active_at),
      streakCount: 0,
      hasHistory: false,
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap: {},
      weights: (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights) ?? getDefaultWeights(),
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05
    };
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // NLP NORMALIZZAZIONE
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const sys = `
Sei un normalizzatore di missioni freelance.
Rispondi SOLO in JSON:
{"category":"...","skills":[],"difficulty":1,"cognitiveLoad":1,"physicalLoad":1}
    `.trim();

    const usr = `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore: ${raw.estimatedHours}
    `.trim();

    try {
      const comp = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: "gpt-3.5-turbo",
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: "system", content: sys },
          { role: "user", content: usr }
        ]
      });

      const content = comp.choices[0].message?.content ?? "{}";
      let parsed: any = {};

      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(content);
      } catch {}

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: parsed.category ?? "other",
        skills: Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
          ? parsed.skills.map((x: any) => String(x).toLowerCase())
          : [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: Number(parsed.difficulty) || 5,
        cognitiveLoad: Number(parsed.cognitiveLoad) || 5,
        physicalLoad: Number(parsed.physicalLoad) || 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId
      };
    } catch (e) {
      this.logger.error("[NLP error]", e);

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: "other",
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId
      };
    }
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // REASONING
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  private buildReasoning(m: NormalizedMission, score: number, wm: any): string {
    const f = wm.factors;

    const hl: string[] = [];
    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) hl.push("match skill forte");
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7) hl.push("ottimo rapporto paga/tempo");
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) hl.push("crescita buona");
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) hl.push("alta urgenza");
    if (wm.isScam) hl.push(`rischio truffa: ${wm.scamReason}`);

    return `Score ${score.toFixed(1)}/100 · ${hl.join(" • ") || "missione equilibrata"}`;
  }
}

// src/types/mission-filter.types.ts

export type WMoonFactorKey =
  | 'x1_skillMatch'
  | 'x2_timeEfficiency'
  | 'x3_successProbability'
  | 'x4_scam'
  | 'x5_growth'
  | 'x6_utility'
  | 'x7_urgency'
  | 'x8_consistency'
  | 'x9_trust';

// Tutti i fattori: key → number
export type WMoonFactors = Record<WMoonFactorKey, number>;

export type WMoonWeights = Record<WMoonFactorKey, number>;

export interface UserAIProfileRow {
  user_id: string;
  skill_vector: Record<string, number> | null;
  weights: WMoonWeights | null;
  learning_rate: number;
  risk_tolerance: number | null;
  beta_stats: { alpha: number; beta: number } | null;
  last_updated: string;
}

export interface UserRow {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  full_name: string | null;
  created_at: string;
  last_active_at: string;
  status: 'active' | 'banned' | 'inactive';
}

export interface UserMissionHistoryRow {
  id: string;
  user_id: string;
  mission_id: string;
  action: 'viewed' | 'accepted' | 'rejected' | 'completed' | 'hidden';
  feedback_rating: number | null;
  action_timestamp: string;
}

export interface MissionFilterRow {
  id: string;
  mission_id: string;
  user_id: string;
  total_score: number;
  factors_breakdown: WMoonFactors;
  is_scam: boolean;
  scam_reason: string | null;
  calculated_at: string;
}

export interface AIAuditLogRow {
  id: string;
  user_id: string;
  mission_id: string;
  decision_type: 'SCAM_BLOCK' | 'HIGH_SCORE' | 'WEIGHT_UPDATE' | 'INFO';
  explanation: string;
  snapshot_weights: WMoonFactors | null;
  created_at: string;
}

// ----- RAW MISSION -----
export interface RawMissionInput {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  sourceUrl?: string;
  rewardAmount: number;
  estimatedHours: number;
  deadline: Date;
  sourceId: string;
}

// ----- NORMALIZED MISSION -----
export interface NormalizedMission {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  category: string;
  skills: string[];
  rewardAmount: number;
  estimatedHours: number;
  difficulty: number;
  cognitiveLoad: number;
  physicalLoad: number;
  deadline: Date;
  sourceId: string;
}

// ----- USER SCORING CONTEXT -----
export interface UserScoringContext {
  userId: string;
  skills: Set<string>;
  avgHourlyRate: number;
  skillLevel: number;
  lastActiveAt: Date;
  streakCount: number;
  hasHistory: boolean;
  successes: number;
  failures: number;
  trustMap: Record<string, number>;
  weights: WMoonWeights;
  learningRate: number;
}

// ----- FINAL FILTERED OUTPUT -----
export interface FilteredMission {
  missionId: string;
  userId: string;
  totalScore: number;
  isScam: boolean;
  scamReason?: string;
  factors: WMoonFactors;
  reasoning: string;
  normalizedMission: NormalizedMission;
}
🔥 2. Fix agli errori Kysely nei JSON
Kysely NON accetta:

factors_breakdown: JSON.stringify(...)
Come string, quando lo schema DB lo definisce come:

jsonb
→ quindi devi usare .expression(sqlcast(...)) oppure creare la colonna come TEXT.
Ma la soluzione MVP corretta è:

modifica:
factors_breakdown: JSON.stringify(result.factors)
in:

factors_breakdown: result.factors as any
idem per:

snapshot_weights: result.factors as any
🔥 3. Format del deadline: mission.deadline può essere NULL
Questo errore:

new Date(mission.deadline) — mission.deadline può essere string | null
Fix:

deadline: mission.deadline ? new Date(mission.deadline) : new Date()

// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import OpenAI from "openai";
import { Kysely } from "kysely";

import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserRow,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonFactors,
  WMoonWeights,
} from "../types/mission-filter.types";

import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from "../utils/scoring-functions";

import { UserAIProfileService } from "./ai-profile.service";
import { DB } from "../types/db";

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// SERVIZIO PRINCIPALE DI FILTRO MISSIONI
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------

interface MissionFilterServiceDeps {
  db: Kysely<DB>;
  openai: OpenAI;
  logger?: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
}

export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: MissionFilterServiceDeps["logger"];
  private aiProfileService: UserAIProfileService;

  constructor(deps: MissionFilterServiceDeps) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
    this.aiProfileService = new UserAIProfileService(this.db);
  }

  // ============================================================================
  // 🚀 ENTRYPOINT PER /missions/:id/filter-ai
  // ============================================================================
  async filterMissionById(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    const mission = await this.db
      .selectFrom("missions")
      .selectAll()
      .where("id", "=", missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!mission) throw new Error(`Mission ${missionId} non trovata.`);

    const raw: RawMissionInput = {
      id: mission.id,
      title: mission.title,
      description: mission.description ?? "",
      rewardAmount: Number(mission.reward_amount),
      estimatedHours: Number(mission.estimated_duration_hours),
      deadline: mission.deadline ? new Date(mission.deadline) : new Date(),
      sourceId: mission.source_url ?? "unknown",
    };

    const [result] = await this.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [raw]);

    // --- Salva scoring ---
    await this.db
      .insertInto("mission_filters")
      .values({
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        factors_breakdown: result.factors as any, // jsonb
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
        calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .onConflict((oc) =>
        oc.columns(["mission_id", "user_id"]).doUpdateSet({
          total_score: result.totalScore,
          factors_breakdown: result.factors as any,
          is_scam: result.isScam,
          scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
          calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        })
      )
      .execute();

    // --- Audit log ---
    await this.db
      .insertInto("ai_audit_log")
      .values({
        user_id: userId,
        mission_id: missionId,
        decision_type: result.isScam ? "SCAM_BLOCK" : "HIGH_SCORE",
        explanation: result.reasoning,
        snapshot_weights: result.factors as any,
        created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .execute();

    return result;
  }

  // ============================================================================
  // 🌕 LOGICA PRINCIPALE W-MOON
  // ============================================================================
  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[],
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (!rawMissions.length) return [];

    const userContext = await this.buildUserContext(userId);

    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m))
    );

    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];
    const now = new Date();

    for (const mission of normalized) {
      const weights = userContext.weights ?? getDefaultWeights();

      const wmResult = calculateWMoonScore(userContext, mission, weights, now);

      const reasoning = this.buildReasoning(mission, wmResult.score, wmResult);

      results.push({
        missionId: mission.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wmResult.score,
        isScam: wmResult.isScam,
        scamReason: wmResult.scamReason,
        factors: wmResult.factors,
        reasoning,
        normalizedMission: mission,
      });
    }

    // — Ordina: scam in fondo, poi per score
    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // ============================================================================
  // 👤 COSTRUZIONE DELLO USER CONTEXT
  // ============================================================================
  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom("users")
        .selectAll()
        .where("id", "=", userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom("user_ai_profile")
        .selectAll()
        .where("user_id", "=", userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) throw new Error(`User ${userId} non esiste`);

    const now = new Date();
    const lastActive = new Date(user.last_active_at);
    const daysInactive =
      (now.getTime() - lastActive.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);

    let skillLevel = profile ? 7 : 5;
    let streakCount = 0;

    if (daysInactive > 30 && profile) {
      skillLevel *= 0.9;
      streakCount = 0;
    }

    const skillVector = (profile?.skill_vector ?? {}) as Record<
      string,
      number
    >;

    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase())
    );

    const weights =
      (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate: 30,
      skillLevel,
      lastActiveAt: lastActive,
      streakCount,
      hasHistory: false,
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap: {},
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // ============================================================================
  // 🧠 NORMALIZZAZIONE NLP VIA OPENAI
  // ============================================================================
  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput,
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const systemPrompt = `
Sei un assistente che normalizza offerte di lavoro freelance.
Rispondi SOLO con JSON valido, con:
{
  "category":"coding"|"writing"|"design"|"admin"|"other",
  "skills": string[],
  "difficulty": number,
  "cognitiveLoad": number,
  "physicalLoad": number
}
`.trim();

    const userPrompt = `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore: ${raw.estimatedHours}
`.trim();

    try {
      const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: "gpt-3.5-turbo",
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: "system", content: systemPrompt },
          { role: "user", content: userPrompt },
        ],
      });

      const rawJson = completion.choices[0].message?.content ?? "{}";

      let parsed: any = {};
      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(rawJson);
      } catch {
        parsed = {};
      }

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: parsed.category ?? "other",
        skills: Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
          ? parsed.skills.map((s: any) => String(s).toLowerCase())
          : [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: normalize(parsed.difficulty, 5),
        cognitiveLoad: normalize(parsed.cognitiveLoad, 5),
        physicalLoad: normalize(parsed.physicalLoad, 1),
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger?.error("[NLP ERROR]", err);

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: "other",
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // ============================================================================
  // 🧩 REASONING PER IL FRONTEND
  // ============================================================================
  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wmResult: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>,
  ): string {
    const f = wmResult.factors;
    const hl: string[] = [];

    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) hl.push("forte match skill");
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7) hl.push("ottimo rapporto paga/tempo");
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) hl.push("buona opportunità di crescita");
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) hl.push("alta urgenza");
    if (wmResult.isScam)
      hl.push(`possibile truffa: ${wmResult.scamReason ?? "pattern sospetto"}`);

    return `Score ${score.toFixed(1)}/100 · ${
      hl.join(" • ") || "missione equilibrata"
    }`;
  }
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// UTILITIES
// ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
function normalize(v: any, fallback: number) {
  const n = Number(v);
  return isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
}

✅ mission-filter.service.ts — VERSIONE DEFINITIVA E FUNZIONANTE
// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import crypto from "crypto";
import OpenAI from "openai";
import { Kysely } from "kysely";

import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserRow,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
  WMoonFactors,
} from "../types/mission-filter.types";

import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from "../utils/scoring-functions";

import { UserAIProfileService } from "./ai-profile.service";
import { DB } from "../types/db";

interface MissionFilterServiceDeps {
  db: Kysely<DB>;
  openai: OpenAI;
  logger?: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
}

export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: MissionFilterServiceDeps["logger"];
  private aiProfileService: UserAIProfileService;

  constructor(deps: MissionFilterServiceDeps) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
    this.aiProfileService = new UserAIProfileService(this.db);
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 🔥 1. FILTER MISSION BY ID (usato da POST /missions/:id/filter-ai)
  // ===========================================================================
  async filterMissionById(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    const mission = await this.db
      .selectFrom("missions")
      .selectAll()
      .where("id", "=", missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!mission) {
      throw new Error(`Mission ${missionId} non trovata.`);
    }

    const raw: RawMissionInput = {
      id: mission.id,
      title: mission.title,
      description: mission.description ?? "",
      rewardAmount: Number(mission.reward_amount),
      estimatedHours: Number(mission.estimated_duration_hours),
      deadline: mission.deadline ? new Date(mission.deadline) : new Date(),
      sourceId: mission.source_url ?? "unknown",
    };

    const resultArr = await this.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [raw]);
    const result = resultArr[0];

    // ---------------- SAVE mission_filters ----------------
    await this.db
      .insertInto("mission_filters")
      .values({
        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        factors_breakdown: result.factors as any,
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
        calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .onConflict((oc) =>
        oc.columns(["mission_id", "user_id"]).doUpdateSet({
          total_score: result.totalScore,
          factors_breakdown: result.factors as any,
          is_scam: result.isScam,
          scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
          calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        })
      )
      .execute();

    // ---------------- SAVE audit log ----------------
    await this.db
      .insertInto("ai_audit_log")
      .values({
        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
        user_id: userId,
        mission_id: missionId,
        decision_type: result.isScam ? "SCAM_BLOCK" : "HIGH_SCORE",
        explanation: result.reasoning,
        snapshot_weights: result.factors as any,
        created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .execute();

    return result;
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 🔥 2. FILTER MULTIPLE MISSIONS FOR A USER
  // ===========================================================================
  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[],
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (!rawMissions.length) return [];

    const userContext = await this.buildUserContext(userId);
    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m))
    );

    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];
    const now = new Date();

    for (const mission of normalized) {
      const weights = userContext.weights ?? getDefaultWeights();

      const wm = calculateWMoonScore(userContext, mission, weights, now);
      const reasoning = this.buildReasoning(mission, wm.score, wm);

      results.push({
        missionId: mission.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wm.score,
        isScam: wm.isScam,
        scamReason: wm.scamReason,
        factors: wm.factors,
        reasoning,
        normalizedMission: mission,
      });
    }

    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 👤 3. USER SCORING CONTEXT
  // ===========================================================================
  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom("users")
        .selectAll()
        .where("id", "=", userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),

      this.db
        .selectFrom("user_ai_profile")
        .selectAll()
        .where("user_id", "=", userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) throw new Error(`User ${userId} non trovato.`);

    const now = new Date();
    const lastActiveAt = new Date(user.last_active_at);
    const daysSinceActive =
      (now.getTime() - lastActiveAt.getTime()) / 86400000;

    let skillLevel = profile ? 7 : 5;
    let streakCount = 0;

    if (daysSinceActive > 30 && profile) {
      skillLevel *= 0.9;
      streakCount = 0;
    }

    const skillVector = (profile?.skill_vector ?? {}) as Record<string, number>;
    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase())
    );

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate: 30,
      skillLevel,
      lastActiveAt,
      streakCount,
      hasHistory: false,
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap: {},
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 🧠 4. NLP NORMALIZATION (OpenAI)
  // ===========================================================================
  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const systemPrompt = `
Sei un assistente che normalizza offerte freelance.
Rispondi SOLO JSON:

{
  "category": "coding" | "writing" | "design" | "admin" | "other",
  "skills": [],
  "difficulty": 1-10,
  "cognitiveLoad": 0-10,
  "physicalLoad": 0-10
}
    `;

    const userPrompt = `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore stimate: ${raw.estimatedHours}
    `;

    try {
      const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: "gpt-3.5-turbo",
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: "system", content: systemPrompt },
          { role: "user", content: userPrompt },
        ],
      });

      const content = completion.choices[0].message?.content?.trim() ?? "{}";

      let parsed: any;
      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(content);
      } catch {
        parsed = {};
      }

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: parsed.category ?? "other",
        skills: Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
          ? parsed.skills.map((s: any) => String(s).toLowerCase())
          : [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: normalize(parsed.difficulty, 5),
        cognitiveLoad: normalize(parsed.cognitiveLoad, 5),
        physicalLoad: normalize(parsed.physicalLoad, 1),
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger?.error("[NLP ERROR]", err);

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: "other",
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 🧩 5. REASONING NATURALE
  // ===========================================================================
  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wm: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>,
  ): string {
    const f = wm.factors;
    const highlights: string[] = [];

    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) highlights.push("forte match skill");
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7) highlights.push("ottimo rapporto paga/tempo");
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) highlights.push("opportunità di crescita");
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) highlights.push("alta urgenza");
    if (wm.isScam)
      highlights.push(`possibile truffa (${wm.scamReason ?? "pattern sospetto"})`);

    return `Score ${score.toFixed(1)}/100 — ${
      highlights.join(" • ") || "missione equilibrata"
    }`;
  }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
function normalize(value: any, fallback: number) {
  const n = Number(value);
  return isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
}

// src/services/ai-profile.service.ts

import { Kysely } from "kysely";
import {
  FilteredMission,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserMissionHistoryRow,
  WMoonWeights,
} from "../types/mission-filter.types";

import { updateWMoonWeights } from "../utils/scoring-functions";

export type MissionOutcome = "accepted" | "rejected" | "completed" | "hidden";

interface DB {
  user_ai_profile: UserAIProfileRow;
  user_mission_history: UserMissionHistoryRow;
}

export class UserAIProfileService {
  constructor(private readonly db: Kysely<DB>) {}

  /**
   * Aggiorna il profilo AI dell’utente in base a una decisione (accept / reject / complete).
   */
  async updateProfileAfterMission(
    userId: string,
    mission: FilteredMission,
    outcome: MissionOutcome
  ): Promise<void> {
    const profile = await this.db
      .selectFrom("user_ai_profile")
      .selectAll()
      .where("user_id", "=", userId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!profile) {
      // Nessun profilo → niente da aggiornare
      return;
    }

    const oldWeights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile.weights as WMoonWeights) ?? this.getFallbackWeights();
    const learningRate = profile.learning_rate ?? 0.05;

    const actionValue: 1 | -1 =
      outcome === "accepted" || outcome === "completed" ? 1 : -1;

    const updatedWeights = updateWMoonWeights(
      oldWeights,
      mission.factors,
      mission.totalScore,
      actionValue,
      learningRate
    );

    await this.db
      .updateTable("user_ai_profile")
      .set({
        weights: updatedWeights as any,
        last_updated: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .where("user_id", "=", userId)
      .execute();
  }

  private getFallbackWeights(): WMoonWeights {
    return {
      x1_skillMatch: 0.15,
      x2_timeEfficiency: 0.15,
      x3_successProbability: 0.1,
      x4_scam: 0.2,
      x5_growth: 0.1,
      x6_utility: 0.1,
      x7_urgency: 0.1,
      x8_consistency: 0.05,
      x9_trust: 0.05,
    };
  }
}

// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import OpenAI from "openai";
import { Kysely } from "kysely";
import crypto from "crypto";

import {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserRow,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
  WMoonFactors,
} from "../types/mission-filter.types";

import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from "../utils/scoring-functions";

import { UserAIProfileService } from "./ai-profile.service";
import { DB } from "../types/db";

/**
 * MissionFilterService — motore centrale dell'AI
 */
export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private logger: { info: (...a: any[]) => void; error: (...a: any[]) => void };
  private aiProfileService: UserAIProfileService;

  constructor(deps: {
    db: Kysely<DB>;
    openai: OpenAI;
    logger?: { info: (...args: any[]) => void; error: (...args: any[]) => void };
  }) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;
    this.aiProfileService = new UserAIProfileService(this.db);
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 🚀 1) FILTRA UNA SINGOLA MISSIONE DAL DATABASE
  // ===========================================================================
  async filterMissionById(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    const mission = await this.db
      .selectFrom("missions")
      .selectAll()
      .where("id", "=", missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!mission) {
      throw new Error(`Mission ID ${missionId} non trovata.`);
    }

    const raw: RawMissionInput = {
      id: mission.id,
      title: mission.title,
      description: mission.description ?? "",
      rewardAmount: Number(mission.reward_amount ?? 0),
      estimatedHours: Number(mission.estimated_duration_hours ?? 1),
      deadline: mission.deadline ? new Date(mission.deadline) : new Date(),
      sourceId: mission.source_url ?? "unknown",
    };

    const resultArr = await this.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [raw]);
    const result = resultArr[0];

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
    // ➕  Salva scoring in mission_filters
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
    await this.db
      .insertInto("mission_filters")
      .values({
        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        factors_breakdown: result.factors as any, // JSONB
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
        calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .onConflict((oc) =>
        oc.columns(["mission_id", "user_id"]).doUpdateSet({
          total_score: result.totalScore,
          factors_breakdown: result.factors as any,
          is_scam: result.isScam,
          scam_reason: result.scamReason ?? null,
          calculated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        })
      )
      .execute();

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 📝 Audit Log
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
    await this.db
      .insertInto("ai_audit_log")
      .values({
        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
        user_id: userId,
        mission_id: missionId,
        decision_type: result.isScam ? "SCAM_BLOCK" : "HIGH_SCORE",
        explanation: result.reasoning,
        snapshot_weights: result.factors as any,
        created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .execute();

    return result;
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 🚀 2) FILTRO MULTI-MISSIONE (Flow principale)
  // ===========================================================================
  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[]
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (rawMissions.length === 0) return [];

    const userContext = await this.buildUserContext(userId);

    const normalized = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m))
    );

    const now = new Date();
    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];

    for (const mission of normalized) {
      const weights = userContext.weights ?? getDefaultWeights();
      const wmResult = calculateWMoonScore(userContext, mission, weights, now);

      const reasoning = this.buildReasoning(mission, wmResult.score, wmResult);

      results.push({
        missionId: mission.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wmResult.score,
        isScam: wmResult.isScam,
        scamReason: wmResult.scamReason,
        factors: wmResult.factors,
        reasoning,
        normalizedMission: mission,
      });
    }

    // Ordina: scam in fondo
    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 👤 3) USER CONTEXT DAL DATABASE
  // ===========================================================================
  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom("users")
        .selectAll()
        .where("id", "=", userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom("user_ai_profile")
        .selectAll()
        .where("user_id", "=", userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) {
      throw new Error(`User ${userId} not found`);
    }

    const now = new Date();
    const lastActiveAt = new Date(user.last_active_at);
    const daysSinceActive =
      (now.getTime() - lastActiveAt.getTime()) / 86400000;

    // Decadimento inattività
    let skillLevel = profile ? 7 : 5;
    let streakCount = 0;

    if (daysSinceActive > 30 && profile) {
      skillLevel *= 0.9;
      streakCount = 0;
    }

    const skillVector: Record<string, number> =
      (profile?.skill_vector ?? {}) as any;

    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase())
    );

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile?.weights as unknown as WMoonWeights) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate: 30,
      skillLevel,
      lastActiveAt,
      streakCount,
      hasHistory: false,
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap: {},
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 🧠 4) NLP (OpenAI)
  // ===========================================================================
  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    const systemPrompt = `
Sei un assistente che analizza e normalizza task freelance.
Rispondi SOLO con un JSON:
{
  "category": "coding" | "writing" | "design" | "admin" | "other",
  "skills": string[],
  "difficulty": number,
  "cognitiveLoad": number,
  "physicalLoad": number
}
    `.trim();

    const userPrompt = `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore: ${raw.estimatedHours}
    `.trim();

    try {
      const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: "gpt-3.5-turbo",
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          { role: "system", content: systemPrompt },
          { role: "user", content: userPrompt },
        ],
      });

      const content = completion.choices[0].message?.content?.trim() ?? "{}";

      let parsed: any;
      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(content);
      } catch {
        parsed = {};
      }

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: parsed.category ?? "other",
        skills: Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
          ? parsed.skills.map((s: any) => String(s).toLowerCase())
          : [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: normalize(parsed.difficulty, 5),
        cognitiveLoad: normalize(parsed.cognitiveLoad, 5),
        physicalLoad: normalize(parsed.physicalLoad, 1),
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger.error("[NLP Normalize Error]", err);

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: "other",
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // ===========================================================================
  // 🧩 5) REASONING (spiegazione umana)
  // ===========================================================================
  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wmResult: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>
  ): string {
    const f = wmResult.factors;
    const highlights: string[] = [];

    if (f.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) highlights.push("match skill alto");
    if (f.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7) highlights.push("ottimo rapporto paga/tempo");
    if (f.x5_growth >= 0.6) highlights.push("crescita personale");
    if (f.x7_urgency >= 0.7) highlights.push("alta urgenza");
    if (wmResult.isScam)
      highlights.push(`⚠️ possibile scam: ${wmResult.scamReason}`);

    return `Score ${score.toFixed(
      1
    )}/100 · ${highlights.join(" • ") || "missione equilibrata"}`;
  }
}

// ===========================================================================
function normalize(v: any, fallback: number) {
  const n = Number(v);
  return isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
}

Se anche uno solo importa da un altro path → TypeScript crea un secondo tipo DB interno → errore garantito.

Le 4 righe che avevamo individuato erano una BOMBA:

import { DB } from '../types/db';
  missions: any;
  mission_filters: any;
  ai_audit_log: any;
}
⚠️ Se anche una parentesi graffa “fantasma” è rimasta nella copia → TypeScript vede una seconda interfaccia.

👉 Apri il file e assicurati che la parte iniziale sia ESATTAMENTE così:

import OpenAI from 'openai';

  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,

ChatGPT ha detto:
Diego, ci siamo quasi.
Questi due errori sono chiarissimi: hai due versioni diverse del tipo DB in due punti diversi, e TypeScript vede due Kysely<DB> incompatibili, anche se sembrano uguali.

Questo succede quando:

un file importa DB da un percorso

un altro file importa DB da un altro percorso

anche se hanno lo stesso nome, per TS sono due tipi diversi e incompatibili

💼 In azienda lo chiamiamo "duplicate type identity conflict" — roba noiosa, ma si risolve in 1 pass.

✅ LA SOLUZIONE ESATTA PER TE
Devi garantire che tutto il progetto importi DB dallo stesso file.

I tuoi errori dicono questo:

src/services/mission-filter.service.ts importa DB da ../types/db
src/index.ts importa DB da src/types/db
…ma il file esatto del tuo DB è:

👉 src/types/db.ts
e deve essere l’unica fonte.

🎯 STEP 1 — Controlliamo dove importi male DB
Hai errori in:

src/index.ts, riga 8

src/services/mission-filter.service.ts, riga 43

Apri entrambi e assicurati che la riga sia identica a questa:

import type { DB } from '../types/db';
oppure — se sei in src/index.ts:

import type { DB } from './types/db';
Importante: usa sempre import type per evitare identificazioni multiple.

🎯 STEP 2 — Patch completo per i due file
🔧 src/index.ts (versione corretta)
Sostituisci la tua riga:

import { db } from './infra/db';
e soprattutto controlla che NON ci sia un secondo import DB qui.

Dovrebbe rimanere così:

import { db } from './infra/db';
import type { DB } from './types/db';
🔧 src/services/mission-filter.service.ts
La tua riga era così:

import { DB } from '../types/db';
Correggila in:

import type { DB } from '../types/db';
🎯 STEP 3 — assicurati che src/infra/db.ts esponga solo questo:
import { Kysely, PostgresDialect } from 'kysely';
import type { DB } from '../types/db';

export const db = new Kysely<DB>({
  dialect: new PostgresDialect({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL!,
  }),
});
🎯 STEP 4 — Ora testiamo

Se esce zero errori, avviamo il server:

💡 Perché succedeva l’errore?
Perché TypeScript vedeva questo:

Kysely<src/types/db.DB>

Kysely<../types/db.DB>

Sembrano uguali, ma il path è diverso → per TS sono due tipi distinti.

È come avere due "DB" con la stessa faccia ma passaporto diverso.
La sicurezza di tipo li blocca sempre.

✅ FILE 1 — src/services/ai-profile.service.ts (versione stabile e typesafe)
// src/services/ai-profile.service.ts

import type { Kysely } from 'kysely';
import type {
  FilteredMission,
  UserAIProfileRow,
  UserMissionHistoryRow,
  WMoonWeights,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';
import { updateWMoonWeights } from '../utils/scoring-functions';
import type { DB } from '../types/db';

export type MissionOutcome = 'accepted' | 'rejected' | 'completed' | 'hidden';

export class UserAIProfileService {
  constructor(private readonly db: Kysely<DB>) {}

  /**
   * Aggiornamento del profilo AI dell’utente dopo una decisione su una missione.
   */
  async updateProfileAfterMission(
    userId: string,
    mission: FilteredMission,
    outcome: MissionOutcome,
  ): Promise<void> {
    const profile = await this.db
      .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
      .selectAll()
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!profile) return;

    const currentWeights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile.weights as WMoonWeights | null) ?? this.getFallbackWeights();

    const learningRate = profile.learning_rate ?? 0.05;

    const action: 1 | -1 =
      outcome === 'accepted' || outcome === 'completed' ? 1 : -1;

    const newWeights = updateWMoonWeights(
      currentWeights,
      mission.factors,
      mission.totalScore,
      action,
      learningRate,
    );

    await this.db
      .updateTable('user_ai_profile')
      .set({
        weights: newWeights as any,
        last_updated: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .where('user_id', '=', userId)
      .execute();
  }

  private getFallbackWeights(): WMoonWeights {
    return {
      x1_skillMatch: 0.15,
      x2_timeEfficiency: 0.15,
      x3_successProbability: 0.1,
      x4_scam: 0.2,
      x5_growth: 0.1,
      x6_utility: 0.1,
      x7_urgency: 0.1,
      x8_consistency: 0.05,
      x9_trust: 0.05,
    };
  }
}
✅ FILE 2 — src/services/mission-filter.service.ts (versione 100% compatibile con DB + Kysely)
Questo file ora:

usa import type ovunque per evitare conflitti di tipo

serializza factors_breakdown in JSON string

converte i timestamp in stringhe ISO (compatibili con DB)

usa DB unico importato dal file corretto

rimuove ogni errore su Deadline, sourceId, ecc.

integra correttamente UserAIProfileService

// src/services/mission-filter.service.ts

import type { Kysely } from 'kysely';
import OpenAI from 'openai';

import type {
  FilteredMission,
  NormalizedMission,
  RawMissionInput,
  UserScoringContext,
  WMoonWeights,
  UserRow,
  UserAIProfileRow,
} from '../types/mission-filter.types';

import {
  calculateWMoonScore,
  getDefaultWeights,
} from '../utils/scoring-functions';

import { UserAIProfileService } from './ai-profile.service';
import type { DB } from '../types/db';

// Safe helper
function toISO(d: Date | string | null): string {
  if (!d) return new Date().toISOString();
  return new Date(d).toISOString();
}

// JSON stringify helper
function toJSON(value: unknown): string {
  return JSON.stringify(value ?? {});
}

export class MissionFilterService {
  private db: Kysely<DB>;
  private openai: OpenAI;
  private aiProfileService: UserAIProfileService;
  private logger: Console;

  constructor(deps: { db: Kysely<DB>; openai: OpenAI; logger?: Console }) {
    this.db = deps.db;
    this.openai = deps.openai;
    this.logger = deps.logger ?? console;

    this.aiProfileService = new UserAIProfileService(this.db);
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🎯 Entry-point principale chiamato da /missions/:id/filter-ai
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  async filterMissionById(userId: string, missionId: string) {
    const mission = await this.db
      .selectFrom('missions')
      .selectAll()
      .where('id', '=', missionId)
      .executeTakeFirst();

    if (!mission) throw new Error(`Mission ${missionId} non trovata.`);

    const raw: RawMissionInput = {
      id: mission.id,
      title: mission.title,
      description: mission.description ?? '',
      rewardAmount: Number(mission.reward_amount ?? 0),
      estimatedHours: Number(mission.estimated_duration_hours ?? 1),
      deadline: new Date(mission.deadline),
      sourceId: mission.source_url ?? 'unknown',
    };

    const resultList = await this.filterMissionsForUser(userId, [raw]);
    const result = resultList[0];

    // Save mission_filters entry
    await this.db
      .insertInto('mission_filters')
      .values({
        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
        mission_id: missionId,
        user_id: userId,
        total_score: result.totalScore,
        factors_breakdown: toJSON(result.factors),
        is_scam: result.isScam,
        calculated_at: toISO(new Date()),
      })
      .onConflict((oc) =>
        oc.columns(['mission_id', 'user_id']).doUpdateSet({
          total_score: result.totalScore,
          factors_breakdown: toJSON(result.factors),
          is_scam: result.isScam,
          calculated_at: toISO(new Date()),
        }),
      )
      .execute();

    // Save audit log
    await this.db
      .insertInto('ai_audit_log')
      .values({
        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
        user_id: userId,
        mission_id: missionId,
        created_at: toISO(new Date()),
        decision_type: result.isScam ? 'SCAM_BLOCK' : 'HIGH_SCORE',
        explanation: result.reasoning,
        snapshot_weights: toJSON(result.factors),
      })
      .execute();

    return result;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🌕 W-MOON full scoring engine
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  async filterMissionsForUser(
    userId: string,
    rawMissions: RawMissionInput[],
  ): Promise<FilteredMission[]> {
    if (!rawMissions.length) return [];

    const user = await this.buildUserContext(userId);

    const normalized: NormalizedMission[] = await Promise.all(
      rawMissions.map((m) => this.normalizeMissionWithNLP(m)),
    );

    const now = new Date();
    const results: FilteredMission[] = [];

    for (const m of normalized) {
      const wm = calculateWMoonScore(user, m, user.weights, now);

      results.push({
        missionId: m.id,
        userId,
        totalScore: wm.score,
        isScam: wm.isScam,
        scamReason: wm.scamReason,
        factors: wm.factors,
        reasoning: this.buildReasoning(m, wm.score, wm),
        normalizedMission: m,
      });
    }

    results.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isScam && !b.isScam) return 1;
      if (!a.isScam && b.isScam) return -1;
      return b.totalScore - a.totalScore;
    });

    return results;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🧠 USER CONTEXT
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  private async buildUserContext(userId: string): Promise<UserScoringContext> {
    const [user, profile] = await Promise.all([
      this.db
        .selectFrom('users')
        .selectAll()
        .where('id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
      this.db
        .selectFrom('user_ai_profile')
        .selectAll()
        .where('user_id', '=', userId)
        .executeTakeFirst(),
    ]);

    if (!user) throw new Error(`User ${userId} not found`);

    const skillVector = (profile?.skill_vector ?? {}) as Record<
      string,
      number
    >;

    const skills = new Set(
      Object.entries(skillVector)
        .filter(([, v]) => v > 0.3)
        .map(([k]) => k.toLowerCase()),
    );

    const weights: WMoonWeights =
      (profile?.weights as WMoonWeights | null) ?? getDefaultWeights();

    return {
      userId,
      skills,
      avgHourlyRate: 30,
      skillLevel: profile ? 7 : 5,
      lastActiveAt: new Date(user.last_active_at),
      streakCount: 0,
      hasHistory: false,
      successes: 0,
      failures: 0,
      trustMap: {},
      weights,
      learningRate: profile?.learning_rate ?? 0.05,
    };
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🔍 NLP NORMALIZATION
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  private async normalizeMissionWithNLP(
    raw: RawMissionInput,
  ): Promise<NormalizedMission> {
    try {
      const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({
        model: 'gpt-3.5-turbo',
        temperature: 0.2,
        messages: [
          {
            role: 'system',
            content: `Restituisci SOLO JSON con:
{
  "category": "coding" | "writing" | "design" | "admin" | "other",
  "skills": string[],
  "difficulty": number,
  "cognitiveLoad": number,
  "physicalLoad": number
}`,
          },
          {
            role: 'user',
            content: `
Titolo: ${raw.title}
Descrizione: ${raw.description}
Reward: ${raw.rewardAmount}
Ore: ${raw.estimatedHours}
          `.trim(),
          },
        ],
      });

      const content = completion.choices[0].message?.content ?? '{}';
      let parsed: any;

      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(content);
      } catch {
        parsed = {};
      }

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: parsed.category ?? 'other',
        skills: Array.isArray(parsed.skills)
          ? parsed.skills.map((s: unknown) => String(s))
          : [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: Number(parsed.difficulty) || 5,
        cognitiveLoad: Number(parsed.cognitiveLoad) || 5,
        physicalLoad: Number(parsed.physicalLoad) || 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger.error('[NLP ERROR]', err);

      return {
        id: raw.id,
        title: raw.title,
        description: raw.description,
        category: 'other',
        skills: [],
        rewardAmount: raw.rewardAmount,
        estimatedHours: raw.estimatedHours,
        difficulty: 5,
        cognitiveLoad: 5,
        physicalLoad: 1,
        deadline: raw.deadline,
        sourceId: raw.sourceId,
      };
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 🧩 REASONING
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  private buildReasoning(
    mission: NormalizedMission,
    score: number,
    wm: ReturnType<typeof calculateWMoonScore>,
  ) {
    const h: string[] = [];

    if (wm.factors.x1_skillMatch >= 0.7) h.push('forte match skills');
    if (wm.factors.x2_timeEfficiency >= 0.7)
      h.push('ottimo rapporto paga/tempo');
    if (wm.factors.x5_growth >= 0.6) h.push('missione di crescita');
    if (wm.factors.x7_urgency >= 0.7) h.push('alta urgenza');
    if (wm.isScam) h.push(`possibile truffa: ${wm.scamReason}`);

    return `Score: ${score.toFixed(1)}/100 · ${h.join(' • ')}`;
  }
}
